Current Affairs Commentary

How to Understand the Tanaka Memorial (2)

Based on Professor Thomas Millard's description of "Japanese Imperialism" quoted in yesterday's commentary, we can understand that Japan's "foreign aggression," particularly its active aggression in Northeast China, is by no means as propagandized by apologists for Japanese imperialism, due to (1) overpopulation and (2) lack of resources. As for the current claims by Japanese militarists and politicians that "Manchuria and Mongolia are Japan's lifeline" and "Manchuria and Mongolia are vital to Japan's national defense," and even the statement by Motoyama Hikoichi, president of the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun, that "Manchuria and Mongolia on the map look like a pistol pointing at Japan's abdomen, which alone is enough to make the Japanese people sleeplessly pay attention to the interests and security of that area" (see a letter from Yamamoto to Harvard, who runs 25 news outlets in the United States, on October 24), these are extremely absurd and unreasonable fallacies. In fact, they adequately demonstrate that Japan is an evil demon trampling on public reason and justice, because "Manchuria and Mongolia" are Chinese territory. There is not a shred of reason to connect them with Japan's "survival," and the act of forcibly claiming a neighboring country's territory as one's own "national defense key area" is absolutely intolerable to public reason and justice. As for saying that "Manchuria and Mongolia on the map look like a pistol pointing at Japan's abdomen," thereby justifying the forcible occupation of "Manchuria and Mongolia," then if the Japanese suddenly have a whim and feel that "the United States on the map looks like a ferocious beast, baring its fangs and claws, lunging at Japan," or suddenly feel that "Soviet Russia on the map is truly like the so-called 'Bear of the East,' constantly posing a serious threat to Japan," wouldn't Japan also have to "sleeplessly pay attention to the interests and security of that area"? At the same time, as the Japanese see it, we can also say that "Japan on the map looks like a silkworm, gnawing along the edge of the Eurasian continent like a mulberry leaf." Then, in fact, countries established on the Eurasian continent will have no choice but to rise up together and destroy Japan. Using some absurd and untenable reason to try to cover up its ambition and atrocities is originally a common trick of general ambitious people, which is not surprising. However, here we should clearly recognize that the various fallacies mentioned above cannot constitute a reason for Japan's foreign aggression and especially its active aggression in Northeast China. Even more, they cannot be regarded as a valid cause for foreign aggression.

If we want to grasp the reasons for Japan's foreign aggression, we must first recognize that Japan is a member of the international capitalist countries. Since the Meiji Restoration, Japan's financial magnates such as the Mitsui and Mitsubishi "kingdoms" have invisibly gained real power to dominate politics. At the same time, they promoted Japan's departure from the ruins of feudalism and embarked on the road of capitalism. The slogan of capitalism in its initial stage was "free competition," but it subsequently transformed into "monopoly" and "exclusive control." What appeared in reality was the overwhelming of general small and medium-sized enterprises domestically, forming organizations such as trusts and syndicates. They monopolized capital and manipulated finance. Abroad, they searched for markets, raw materials, and investment destinations, and began an economic competition with other capitalist countries, further deeply planting the roots of poisoning weak nations. When capitalism gradually developed to its peak, it formed imperialism, which possessed extremely brutal forms. Domestically, it suppressed reactionary forces with violence, and further used slogans such as "promoting national prestige" and "expanding influence" to deceive the people, so that they would willingly die for it. Abroad, it began military competition and violent aggression, and ultimately stirred up a black tide of terror and misery in a peaceful and tranquil world. Especially Japan, when she began to embark on the road of capitalism, the capitalism of the West had grown and matured. As soon as she was reborn, she encountered a formidable enemy. Therefore, in the early stages of its growth, it carried an extremely brutal form, holding militarism and using force to challenge the world and compete with the great powers.

At the beginning of the Meiji Restoration, the capitalist class, militarists, bureaucrats, and rulers of Japan established the ocean policy and continental policy for foreign expansion, which is the so-called "legacy of the Meiji Emperor." The outbreak of the two Sino-Japanese and Russo-Japanese Wars was the implementation of the so-called "legacy of the Meiji Emperor." The annexation of Ryukyu, Taiwan, and Korea was precisely the first step in the success of the "Meiji legacy." After the annexation of Ryukyu and Taiwan, the foundation of the ocean policy was established. After this, it focused all its efforts on the realization of its continental policy. Tanaka's foundation for an active policy toward Manchuria and Mongolia was built on the Meiji legacy. It is a consistent development and a consistent advancement, not accidental and not without reason.

The famous Japanese economist Takahashi Kamekichi said in his article "Sino-Japanese Economic Relations and the Policy of Force Toward China," "In fact, Japanese imperialism has always been criticized by public opinion, and yet it still has to use the old tune of the policy of force to maintain its status as a first-class power. The fundamental reason is nothing more than that it cannot expect the development of its imperialism by economic power alone." Similarly, the Japanese political commentator Suzuki Mosaburo also said in his article "The Union of Japanese National Capital and Zaibatsu Capital in China," "In China, first are the Japanese prostitutes, second are the traffickers of high-grade morphine, and third are the salesmen of Mitsui Bussan Co., all advancing fiercely into the Chinese hinterland under the Japanese flag." These statements fully explain the reasons for Japan's foreign aggression by force. Furthermore, they fully prove the pervasiveness of the Japanese imperialists' aggression against China. At the same time, it is precisely to explain how Japanese militarists and bureaucrats are actively implementing the "legacy of the Meiji Emperor."

Although Tanaka Giichi regarded the China issue as his lifelong ambition and was an ambitious militarist, he was by no means as criticized by his Seiyukai party, "Tanaka's head is a bit strange, doing things that common sense cannot imagine." He was only a loyal executor of the Meiji legacy. He was just a reactionary and ambitious militarist. It was also no accident that the memorial for the active policy toward Manchuria and Mongolia was presented by Tanaka.

We must understand the above explanation in order to grasp why Japanese imperialists carried out foreign aggression and why the Tanaka Memorial was produced. At the same time, we can understand the essence of the Tanaka Memorial and the great conspiracy of Tanaka to harm the world.

Shuncheng Wang Mansion Meeting

Foreign Troops Assist in Maintaining Traffic between Beijing and Tianjin

(Beiping) This morning, the Shuncheng Wang Mansion held an emergency meeting. All personnel above the rank of director attended. It was decided to urgently transfer Wan Fulin's troops stationed in Langfang, Yu Zhaolin's 30th Brigade, and Yao Dongfan's one brigade to Tianjin to maintain order. If rioters cause trouble again, they will be stopped. (9th Dispatch)

(Beiping) This morning, two Japanese soldiers went to the vicinity of the Shuncheng Wang Mansion to inquire about news, but were rejected by the guards with a peaceful attitude. (9th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Vice-Zhang urgently telegraphed the Central Government, reporting the truth of the Japanese military's disturbance in Tianjin, and immediately submitted it to the League of Nations, requesting a fair sanction. (9th Dispatch)

National Important News Three

Doihara's Mission to Tianjin

(Beiping) Doihara's original purpose in coming to Tianjin was: (1) To encourage Puyi to organize the Mingguang Empire, which has failed; (2) To collude with disgruntled military officers from Shandong and Shanxi provinces to disturb order. Vice-Zhang has telegraphed the authorities of each province to pay special attention; (3) To plan an attack on Jinzhou; (4) To conspire to disturb Tianjin, Beiping, Zhangjiakou, and Tangshan, creating terror to use as an excuse to advance troops.

Several Japanese Planes Dropped Bombs in Sanjianfang

All Japanese Troops in Shenyang Advanced Towards Northern Manchuria

(Nanjing) The diplomatic circle received a telegram from Beiping on the 9th stating that at 8:00 a.m. on the 8th, several Japanese planes dropped many bombs on the positions of our army in Sanjianfang, Heilongjiang Province. At 10:30 a.m., a Japanese plane went to Heilongjiang's provincial capital, circling for about half an hour. In addition, the Japanese side transferred troops stationed in Korea to Shenyang, and all the troops stationed in Shenyang advanced towards northern Manchuria. The majority of the troops arrived at Jiangqiao on the 7th, and they still actively planned to invade Heilongjiang. (9th Dispatch)

(Tokyo) This station has just received a telegram from a reporter stating that Ma Zhanshan has already declared war. Ma's troops retreated after fighting with Japanese soldiers in Nenjiang. According to a telegram from Shenyang, Ma Zhanshan has telegraphed Zhang Xueliang to transfer Jilin troops to help resist Japan. The above news has not been officially verified. (9th Reuters Dispatch)

(Tokyo) According to the report received by the Army Ministry today, the Manchurian situation is once again in crisis. It is reported that Chinese troops are now concentrated south of Angangxi, which is about twenty miles north of the Japanese troop line in Taonan. It is also reported that there are a total of 5,600 Chinese infantry soldiers, 2,400 cavalry soldiers, and 300 artillery and engineering soldiers, while there are less than 1,000 Japanese soldiers. The number of reinforcements in Taonan is not large, because the reinforcements that were transferred before stopped advancing on the 6th of this month and returned to Changchun. (9th Reuters Dispatch)

The League of Nations Will Announce Japan's Violation of the Charter

The Council Has the Right to Expel Japan

The Recall of Envoys Has Been Discussed Once

(Geneva) People in the League of Nations, regarding Japan's threat to withdraw from the League of Nations, stated that after the Council reopens on the 16th, it will announce that Japan has violated the League of Nations Charter. In this way, the Council has the right to vote to expel Japan. Regarding Japan's claim that the League of Nations is trying to become a "supreme state," people in the League of Nations solemnly stated that the Council's measures regarding the Liaoning-Jilin dispute that are binding on member states to date are only the resolution of September 30, and Japan personally voted in favor of that resolution through Yoshizawa. It was also said that Japan is now demanding that China give written consent to the five basic points proposed by Shidehara before withdrawing its troops, which is enough to prove that the Japanese military's stationing in the three eastern provinces is no longer intended to protect Japanese residents, but to occupy by force instead of the peaceful methods stipulated by the League of Nations Charter and force China to concede. Japan's position is tantamount to admitting that it has violated the League of Nations Charter, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and the Nine-Power Treaty. The statement issued by League of Nations Secretary-General Drummond regarding the Sino-Japanese dispute has aroused commentary here today, believing that Mr. Drummond's opinion has no impact because he has no voting rights and only serves as a messenger between the councilors. The councilors will act on their own. (8th Reuters Dispatch)

(Geneva) There is much speculation about what action the League of Nations Administrative Council will take on the Manchurian issue at the next meeting, but Reuters dares to say that there is absolutely no knowledge here of what kind of resolution the Administrative Council will have. If the Japanese troops still do not withdraw by November 16, a serious warning will be sent to Japan. This is obvious, but even Councilor Briand, including members of the Administrative Council, still does not know what kind of resolution the Administrative Council will have. (8th Reuters Dispatch)

(Geneva) The officialdom here has not heard of the suggestion to recall foreign ambassadors stationed in Tokyo, but admits that all countries have discussed this. Today, a certain League of Nations official told a Reuters reporter that he could not confirm the news that Chairman Briand and other members had discussed the recall of ambassadors stationed in Japan, because Japan refused to comply with the resolutions of the Administrative Council. It is said that the Administrative Council will decide to withdraw diplomatic representatives stationed in Japan when it meets on the 16th, and then adjourn the meeting for a week or ten days to observe the effectiveness of this warning. If recalling envoys still cannot make Japan change its attitude, the Administrative Council will meet again and invoke Article 11 of the League of Nations Charter, which China is now using to request, or Article 15 of the Charter, to declare an economic severance of relations with Japan. The United States' participation in this boycott requires the consent of its Congress, which is currently in recess and will not meet until December 7. The above suggestions to withdraw diplomatic representatives and sever economic relations with Japan are still just empty talk. The current situation is urgent, so it is no wonder that various rumors and speculations arise. (8th Reuters Dispatch)

(Paris) Well-informed sources here believe that the League of Nations Administrative Council may not take extreme measures such as recalling ambassadors stationed in Japan regarding the Manchurian issue. Although idealists in Geneva are spreading alarming rumors, no formal proposal for this step has been made. There is a need to continue exchanging opinions before dealing with the situation, but extreme measures such as the sanctions stipulated in Article 16 of the League of Nations Charter are not an issue. Although legally speaking, war is now going on in Manchuria, neither China nor Japan has mentioned the use of sanctions. (9th Reuters Dispatch)

The Japanese Government's Reply to Briand

Using the Excuse of Repairing the Jiangqiao Bridge to Evade Responsibility for the Challenge

(Tokyo) The Japanese government's response to Briand's note of the 6th regarding the Nenjiang incident was sent to Ambassador Yoshizawa by telegram yesterday morning with instructions to convey it to Briand, and was announced by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at 7:00 p.m. yesterday. The main points are as follows: The cause of the current conflict between the Chinese and Japanese armies is that a small unit of the Japanese army escorted engineers to Nenjiang to repair the railway bridge. However, the Heilongjiang army stationed on the north bank of Nenjiang suddenly opened fire. The Tao'ang Railway was built by the South Manchuria Railway and handed over to China in 1927. However, China has not paid the expenses to date and is unwilling to include it in the loan. Therefore, although the railway has been handed over to China, it can in fact be regarded as the property of the South Manchuria Railway and is one of the railway's feeder lines. The Japanese consul stationed in Qiqihar, in order to protect the interests of the South Manchuria Railway, has repeatedly negotiated with China since mid-October to repair the bridge. However, the Chinese authorities adopted a policy of procrastination and did not allow Japan's request. Recently, the freezing period of Nenjiang is approaching, and there is fear that it will not be able to be repaired. Therefore, the Japanese army decided to escort the engineers of the South Manchuria Railway to carry out the bridge repair. First, in order to avoid conflict, the Japanese consul and the staff officer of the Kwantung Army requested the Heilongjiang provincial authorities to withdraw the Heilongjiang army 10 kilometers back from the north bank of Nenjiang. However, the Heilongjiang army had not withdrawn by November 4, and when the Japanese army arrived near Jiangqiao, it suddenly began shelling. The Japanese army temporarily retreated, and after reinforcements arrived, it repelled the Heilongjiang army at noon on the 6th. The purpose of the Japanese army's dispatch this time is as described above, which is to escort the bridge repair work. However, due to the untrustworthy behavior of the Chinese troops, it had no choice but to take an offensive attitude. The Central Army Headquarters has ordered the commander of the army not to expand military operations any further. (9th Japan United Press Dispatch)

(Paris) Japanese representative Yoshizawa notified Briand today that the Japanese army cannot withdraw from the South Manchuria Railway concession at this time. Yoshizawa was replying to a recent letter from Briand, in which he repeatedly stated that Japan cannot withdraw its troops at this time because China has not yet guaranteed law and order within the territory of the three eastern provinces. (8th Kuomintang Dispatch)

The Japanese Government Will Protest to the League of Nations

Believing that the Secretariat Is Gradually Becoming a Chinese Propaganda Bureau

(Tokyo) According to reliable sources, the Japanese government will instruct Yoshizawa to protest to League of Nations Administrative Council Chairman Briand or to Secretary-General Drummond, opposing the League of Nations' gradual transformation into a Chinese propaganda bureau and its unsatisfactory methods of spreading anti-Japanese air, pointing out that League of Nations Health Bureau representative in China, Dr. Rajchman, and Chinese Finance Minister Song Ziwen live together at the Shanghai Eurasia Radio Station, and the radio station often sends Chinese propaganda texts to the League of Nations. Japan also accused the League of Nations Secretariat of hastily disseminating Chinese propaganda without verifying its words. Japan also said that according to reliable sources, Dr. Rajchman, with the assistance of former League of Nations Secretary Watson, has spent no less than 120,000 yuan on telegram fees to the League of Nations in several weeks. The Japanese protest will also strongly criticize the irresponsible behavior of the League of Nations Secretariat in spreading the news that the great powers may withdraw their diplomatic representatives stationed in Japan. The protest will also state that, in the view of the Japanese, the League of Nations Secretariat has no right to disseminate the unverified reports sent to the League of Nations by the Chinese during the recess of the Administrative Council, because Japan has not reported false and incomplete shocking rumors to the League of Nations. (9th Reuters Dispatch)

Secret Diplomacy between the United States and Japan

The Recommendation Documents Have Not Been Published

(Tokyo) Regarding the Manchurian case, Japan is willing to accept the recommendations of the League of Nations, but cannot be directed by the League of Nations. Today, it seems that both political and non-political circles in Tokyo share this sentiment. In addition to criticizing the League of Nations for credulously believing China's reports, Japan's resentment towards the League of Nations is deepening because the League of Nations Secretariat now values the consequences of the Sino-Japanese dispute and undervalues the cause of the Sino-Japanese dispute. Therefore, it seems that there is no doubt that Japan would rather withdraw from the League of Nations than submit to the orders of the League of Nations, because the Japanese view submission as related to its survival. Japan is now also gradually showing anxiety about so-called secret diplomacy, and is paying special attention to the official document delivered by the US Ambassador to Japan to the Japanese Foreign Minister on November 5. The content of the document has not been published in accordance with the understanding between the two countries. Japan's reply has already been drafted and will probably be sent out tonight. Its content will also not be published, but it is currently believed that its nature is mostly the same as the document replying to Briand on October 29. Political circles are very dissatisfied with this kind of secret official document, because they fear that it will cause alarming rumors outside. It is said that the Japanese government intends to ask the United States to allow its publication. Political circles also said that the behavior of secret diplomacy is very beneficial to China. (9th Reuters Dispatch)

The Shenyang Pseudo-Joint Committee Will Hold a Reorganization Meeting

(Beiping) The Shenyang Joint Committee will hold a reorganization meeting. The local maintenance committee will allocate 300,000 yuan for political expenses. Kan Zhaoxi is willing to take the post of Qingxiang Superintendent, and it is said that Zhao Enzhen and Mu Chun will be in charge of handling the affairs. (9th Dispatch)

Various British Newspaper Views

London, the British "Hueiwen" newspaper's editorial this morning said, "In the confusing reports, one thing is very clear, that is, Japan is denying war on the one hand and carrying out war on the other. We do not say that China is justified, but Japan's continued pursuit of its current methods is truly unreasonable." The "Morning Post", which has a pro-Japanese color, said, "It is doubtful whether the intervention of the League of Nations can truly help pacifism." The "Daily Express" said, "A country that has suffered many earthquakes cannot be shaken by the thunder of Geneva." The "Daily Mail" advocated not being involved in the Manchurian affair. (9th Reuters Dispatch)

Ma Zhanshan Telegraphed that Japanese Troops Invaded the Territory

Longjiang Ma Zhanshan's circular telegram said, "All newspaper offices, elders and brothers throughout the country, please be aware that after the Liaoning and Jilin changes, the Japanese used various methods to collude with bandits, Mongolian bandits, and bad elements to plot against northern Manchuria, using the name of Chinese independence to secretly carry out their ambition to invade land and political power. The Jiang Province is far from the border and is doing its best to defend itself. However, the Japanese blatantly came forward on the 1st of the month, using the excuse of repairing the Nenjiang River Bridge to escort Zhang Haipeng's army from Taonan across the river with Japanese soldiers, oppressing our defense area and launching an attack. In the past two days, the Japanese used eight aircraft and more than 20 cannons to fiercely encircle and attack, and the situation is that they will not stop until they directly attack the provincial capital of Jiang Province. In addition, the Nenjiang River Bridge belongs to our country. What right does Japan have to interfere? Zhanshan originally believed that the League of Nations had a solution to this matter and insisted on avoiding conflict, but the Japanese ignored world peace and consistently pursued their ambition to invade Manchuria and Mongolia. The Jiang Province is in a position of having no choice but to fight with force in order to urgently defend itself. A major disaster is imminent, and the country is about to perish. We can only temper the troops under our command and swear to resist to the death, and we will not hesitate to make all sacrifices. We earnestly ask the elders throughout the country to work hard and cheer up to save the country from danger. I am extremely indignant. Acting Chairman of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government Ma Zhanshan, pressed with a fish seal." (7th Dispatch)

Japanese Troops Again Assisted Bandits in Disturbing Western Liaoning

(Beiping) After the destruction of the bandit troops of Ling Yinqing, who were assisted by the Japanese army, the Japanese secretly ordered Wang Dianzhong to organize the Far East People's Self-Defense Army, with Luo Jiutian as the Chief of Staff and Jin Wutang and Tang Chengtian as Staff Officers. According to Japanese propaganda, the bandit army has Cui Baoshan near Xinmintun as the First Army, with 5,000 bandits; Zhang Xuecheng and Du Tianyi in Liaozhong as the Second Army, with 2,000 bandits; Xiao Mengxiu in Kangping, west of the Liao River, as the Third Army, with 2,000 bandits; and a certain bandit leader in Beizhen, north of Goubangzi, as the Fourth Army, with 4,000 bandits, totaling 13,000 people. The Japanese also propagandized that the bandit army is jointly organized by Mongolian Living Buddhas, Mongolian soldiers, White Russians, and Manchus, consisting of seven ethnic groups. After the armies have finished their liaison, Wang Dianzhong will issue a declaration and start attacking Jinzhou. The First Army will advance westward along the Beining Road after occupying Xinmintun, the Second Army will advance from Liaozhong and Tai'an, the Third Army will advance from Kangping, and the Fourth Army will advance from Beizhen to concentrate and attack Goubangzi. This is what the Japanese have spread and has yet to be verified, but our country has no choice but to make full preparations. (9th Dispatch)

Jiangsu and Nanjing were recommended to draft the budget of the association, 3. Tianjin and Shanghai were recommended as commissioners to receive the seals, documents, etc. of the assembly. (9th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Anti-Japanese Salvation Association of all circles in the capital sent a good telegram to Vice-Zhang: "Japanese soldiers are attacking Heilongjiang on a large scale, and the situation is critical. Please quickly send troops to reinforce and protect our territory." It also telegraphed Ma Zhanshan, Chairman of Heilongjiang: "Your subordinates led the generals and soldiers to loyally and bravely kill the enemy, and the whole country admires them. I hereby send a telegram of condolence, and I still hope that you will work hard to fight and eliminate the bandits and glorify our Chinese people." (9th Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) The telegraph paper of the Guangdong Radio Bureau often prints sentences such as "Swear to avenge the national humiliation, reject enemy goods, persevere to the end, and never forget." When the Japanese Consul Suma saw it, he sent a letter to the municipal government, saying that these sentences clearly refer to anti-Japanese sentiment and are really difficult to tolerate. He hoped to find a way to stop them. The municipal government replied with a letter refuting it, saying that this is a patriotic act and is just a vague expression, which is difficult to interfere with. (9th Dispatch)

The Special Foreign Affairs Committee Held a Meeting

(Nanjing) The Special Foreign Affairs Committee held a meeting at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at 6:00 p.m. on the 9th, attended by Yu Youren, Shao Yuanchong, Kong Xiangxi, He Yaozu, Wu Tiecheng, Chen Bulei, Chen Shaokuan, Li Jinlun, etc., to discuss the riot in Tianjin. Yesterday's Central Executive Committee Held an Extraordinary Plenary Meeting

The Presidium of the Fourth Plenary Session is Set at Seven Members, Five Already Nominated, Remaining Two to be Nominated by Representatives; Ye Chucang Remains Secretary-General of the Congress

(Nanjing) The Third Central Executive Committee held an extraordinary plenary meeting in the first conference hall of the Central Party Headquarters at 10:00 AM on the 9th. Organizational Regulations of the Reception Committee Promulgated

(Nanjing) The National Government promulgated on the 9th the organizational regulations for the Committee for Receiving Matters in the Northeast Regions: 1. This committee shall, under the order of the National Government, discuss and decide on the details of receiving the Northeast regions occupied by the Japanese army, and handle the reception and rehabilitation matters in those regions. 2. This committee shall be organized by seven members appointed by the National Government, and one member shall be designated as the chairman, who shall be responsible for all affairs of the committee. 3. This committee shall have the following departments: (1) Political Affairs Department, (2) Foreign Affairs Department, (3) Security Department, (4) Transportation Department. 4. The Political Affairs Department shall be in charge of civil affairs, finance, financial industry, and industry in the received areas. 5. The Foreign Affairs Department shall be in charge of contacting and negotiating with representatives sent by various governments, deciding on the details of receiving and withdrawing areas, and foreign affairs related to the above matters. 6. The Security Department shall be in charge of the army, military police, police, and their deployment and supervision, as well as security matters in the received areas. 7. The Transportation Department shall be in charge of railways, highways, telecommunications, telephones, and all other transportation matters. 8. Each department shall have a director, appointed by the National Government, who may be concurrently held by a committee member. 9. This committee shall have a secretary-general, appointed by the National Government, who shall, under the direction of the chairman, be in charge of the administrative matters of the committee and matters assigned by the chairman. 10. This committee may have counselors to assist in the committee's affairs, appointed by the National Government. 11. The number, appointment, removal, and job allocation methods of this committee's staff shall be determined separately. 12. This committee may, when necessary, hire Chinese and foreign experts as specialist members to handle or design various matters. 13. This committee shall, regarding the progress of various matters designated in the resolutions of the League of Nations, invite representatives sent by various governments to observe, and shall provide them with all conveniences. This committee shall at any time prepare a reception record and submit it to the representatives sent by various governments for reference. 14. After this committee receives various organs in the received areas, it shall immediately request the National Government to appoint responsible personnel to restore administrative organs and local order. 15. This committee may, when necessary, declare martial law in the received areas in accordance with the law. 16. The amendment of these regulations shall be carried out by order of the National Government. 17. These regulations shall be promulgated and implemented by the National Government. (Special dispatch on the 9th)

(Beijing) Gu Weijun and Liu Zhe will postpone their trip to Beijing due to the Tianjin incident. (Special dispatch on the 9th)

Important Foreign Telegrams

International Chamber of Commerce Silver Expert Committee Issues Report

▲ Reuters, London, 9th: The Silver Expert Committee dispatched by the International Chamber of Commerce to consider whether immediate international action could improve the status of silver has today issued its report. The report advocates for the establishment of a more stable position for silver prices, a higher market price, and the conclusion of a sales contract between North American silver miners and the Indian government. The report states that China has suffered greatly in recent years, but the fall in silver prices is only one of the reasons. Indeed, China is the only country in the world where prices and daily life change the least. Although the Chinese government intends to adopt the gold standard, silver will remain the main standard of Chinese currency for many years to come. The committee now believes that China can still bear a gradual and steady increase in the gold value of its currency, but the increase should not be too large or too fast. This year's silver production is estimated to total 200 million ounces, worth approximately US$56 million. If a group in the United States and the Indian Treasury can negotiate a contract, allowing participants to allocate a considerable amount of silver for sale in the world, it can maintain silver prices at a level that is not detrimental to both buyers and sellers. As silver prices rise, Chinese exchange rates will also rise accordingly. Any significant increase will reduce China's exports and increase its imports. This will benefit those exporting to China, but the amount of silver included in the increased imports into China cannot be predetermined. Supplying it sequentially at a reasonable price will maintain the demand for silver. Therefore, a sudden or excessive rise in silver prices should be avoided. Prematurely determining the price to be achieved is also a major mistake. Therefore, North American silver miners and smelters should negotiate sales contracts with the Indian government. Sales contracts without the participation of the Indian government will not be effective. It is hoped that the Indian government will agree not to sell its silver reserves except at prices higher than those set for silver producers. This section is extremely unfair and is bound to fail. Several parties should work together. The contract should naturally stipulate that any participant may withdraw from the contract, either temporarily or permanently, after any agreed notice period. However, silver may not be sold independently until the contract expires. The report recommends that using silver as part of the reserve for paper currency can reduce the risk of gold shortages. The report does not recommend stipulating the ratio of gold to silver prices, but argues that any government that cannot obtain enough gold to meet its needs should consider purchasing some silver and issuing smaller denomination banknotes, with silver reserves equivalent to the full value of the gold coins replaced. This type of banknote, along with banknotes partially backed by gold, would circulate simultaneously, thereby expanding the basis of credit through the authority of the government. Silver can often be purchased at a low price, so the benefits of silver are endless. The committee believes that the International Chamber of Commerce should urge governments to restore the pre-war fineness of subsidiary coinage, which would restore confidence in the value of silver worldwide. The committee ultimately advocates studying new uses for silver to increase silver sales.

International Clearing Bank Decides to Initiate a Reparations Conference

▲ Guomin News Agency, Basel, Switzerland, 8th: The informal meeting of the Board of Directors of the International Clearing Bank passed a resolution today to convene a new reparations conference. According to the most reliable sources, the new reparations conference can be organized in approximately three weeks to sixty days. Furthermore, according to the provisions of the recent talks between French Prime Minister Laval and U.S. President Hoover, the new reparations conference will take the form of a special advisory committee to engage in the work of reparations revision and war debt restructuring. The location of the meeting has not yet been decided, but it is said that it will not be held in Basel. Currently, the French side is quite willing to convene the meeting as soon as possible, while the German side is not in a hurry, because the German side is eager to find out what specific benefits the meeting will bring to Germany.

Important News

The Japanese Army's Ravaging of Liaodong Province

A correspondent from Beiping reports: The old eastern border region of Liaoning Province includes twenty counties: Andong, Xinbin, Tonghua, Fengcheng, Kuandian, Huanren, Linjiang, Ji'an, Changbai, Antu, Fusong, Fushun, Benxi, Hailong, Huinan, Liuhe, Jin County, Fuxian, Xiuyan, and Zhuanghe. During this incident, except for Andong, where news is easily disseminated due to convenient transportation and is occasionally seen in domestic newspapers, the situation in other counties under the ravages of the brutal Japanese army is rarely recorded in newspapers both north and south. It is as if the Japanese army has not taken any action against the eastern Liaoning counties. In reality, this is due to inconvenient transportation and isolated news. The killings by the brutal Japanese army are no less severe than in the Shenyang-Jilin area. The following is based on a conversation with a gentleman who recently arrived in Beiping from Shanchengzi (the garrison of the Eastern Border Defense Commissioner) and is presented as an introduction (the following is the gentleman's account):

"The eastern border region encompasses twenty counties and is the most resource-rich area in the entire province. Products such as ginseng, deer antlers, soybeans, and timber are among the most significant specialties. However, for more than a decade, it has been plagued by rampant bandits, and the people have lived in abject poverty. The great prosperous area has almost become a bandit world. Since the reorganization of the Northeast Army in the winter of the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, the Eastern Border Defense Commissioner Yu Zhishan has led his troops to be stationed there, overseeing the suppression of bandits. For the past three years, the roots have gradually been eradicated, and the notorious bandit area has begun to transform into a peaceful homeland. However, the September 18th Incident suddenly broke out. On the afternoon of the 19th, Shanchengzi received news that the Japanese army had occupied Shenyang and Changchun. The residents were extremely panicked upon hearing this news. While they were discussing it, the sound of Japanese aircraft whirring had already arrived from the direction of Panshi (belonging to Jilin) and flew over Chaoyangzhen and Hailong towards Changchun. Subsequently, an inquiry was made by the town government via long-distance telephone, and it was learned that five heavy bombs had been dropped in the Panshi County market, killing three farmers and workers and injuring five. Three bombs were dropped in Hailong, killing one police chief and injuring four farmers, as well as destroying one telephone. Three bombs were dropped in Chaoyangzhen, all landing in open areas, fortunately without injuring anyone. Leaflets were also scattered in Panshi, generally stating, 'The Japanese army's dispatch of troops this time is indeed due to China destroying its South Manchuria Railway, leaving it no choice but to defend itself. Merchants and residents should not be alarmed,' and other various divisive words. On the afternoon of the 21st, news of the fall of Jilin was received. From that day onward, Japanese aircraft bombed and reconnoitered important towns and cities along the Shenyang-Hailong and Jilin-Hailong routes every day. Unresisting civilians died under the bombs. According to known information, in addition to the aforementioned Panshi and other counties, Shanchengzi suffered four farmers killed and five injured by bombing. In Qingyuan County, three people were killed and five injured. In Yinggemen, one passenger on a train was killed, one railway policeman was injured, and one passenger car was destroyed. In Yingpanjie, two farmers were injured. In Yantongshan, one merchant was killed and three injured. The number of other unknown casualties is still unknown. On the afternoon of October 2nd, a telephone call was received from the village chief of Xinglongtai, about seventy li west of Shanchengzi, stating that more than a thousand Japanese soldiers allied with bandits had arrived at Dagujiazi, about ten li west of the village, at 2 PM and were camping there. They searched for civilian self-defense firearms and arrested village chief Guo, severely interrogating him before shooting him. They also buried two villagers alive because they were suspected of harboring resentment against Korean residents. Furthermore, there was news that the army would advance towards Shanchengzi the next day. Upon receiving this alarming news, various legal entities feared that Garrison Commander Yu Zhishan had received orders not to resist and retreat. If the Japanese army were to enter and bandits took the opportunity to rise up, the eastern border would be even more unbearable. They immediately contacted nearby towns and cities by telephone, inquiring with the Japanese consulates stationed in each location about the purpose of the Japanese army's arrival. If they were coming to seize territory, then they would have to endure being trampled upon. If they claimed to be protecting Japanese and Korean residents, then the lives and property of Japanese and Korean residents in the eastern border counties had never been in danger. If the Japanese army came, it would arouse public resentment and perhaps turn it against the residents. After repeated negotiations, the Japanese consuls repeatedly stated that they could understand but refused to guarantee to the Japanese army and prevent their advance. On the morning of the 3rd, gentlemen from various towns and cities near Shanchengzi were invited by the Japanese consul to gather at the Shanchengzi railway station and board a train to the Caozhi railway station, about forty li west of Shanchengzi, intending to dissuade them."

Page 9

Summary of Important News

"The Japanese army advancing eastward from Dagujiazi simultaneously received a telephone call from the Shenyang-Hailong Railway Bureau, stating that a combined force of infantry, cavalry, and artillery, numbering approximately one thousand, was traveling eastward from Shenyang this morning at 6 AM on three trains, with an armored car protecting the front, and seemed to be spying on the movements of the Northeast Armies retreating from the east of the province, claiming to be reconnoitering. Upon hearing this alarming news, the gentlemen and representatives of the legal entities invited the Japanese consul to go to Yingpan to dissuade them. Upon arriving at Yingpan, the Japanese consul inquired by telephone where the Japanese army had arrived and received a reply that they had arrived at Qiandian. They then requested the Japanese consul to contact the Japanese army commander by telephone, confirming that the Japanese and Korean residents were not in any danger, and arranged for the commander to meet at Yingpan railway station to state this in person. The Japanese commander agreed not to advance further and telegraphed the troops advancing eastward from Xinglongtai to retreat at the same time. As a result, the eastern border regions have been able to barely maintain peace until now. However, the Japanese are actively carrying out actions to incite the independence of various counties. Maintenance societies have already been established in Fushun, Benxi, and Andong. Furthermore, the Japanese army has sent people to request an audience with Yu Zhishan three times, requesting him to lead his troops to withdraw, but Yu has avoided meeting them. The reason why the Japanese army does not dare to take active action is not because they fear Yu Zhishan, nor because they love the people of the eastern border regions. It is said that because the Japanese army's ambition lies in northern Manchuria, most of the large forces have already gone north, believing that the eastern border counties are already turtles in a jar and fish in a cauldron, and they can come back later and settle them with a proclamation. Therefore, the people of the eastern border regions will still be able to steal a moment of respite for a while," (Morning of the 8th of the 11th month).

Japanese Army's Violent Inspection of Mail and Telegraphs in Shenyang

▲Intended to prevent the leakage of violent acts▲But the fact is that attempts to cover up the truth are futile

"The Shanghai Evening Post" reports that the strictness of the Japanese military officers' censorship of news related to the Liaoning-Jilin Incident is almost the same as during the European War. This newspaper has obtained concrete evidence sufficient to prove the excessive detail of the Japanese censorship. Many of the telegrams sent by this newspaper's correspondent in Shenyang have been completely withheld by the Japanese, and the rest have often been deleted and altered, often losing the original meaning of the text. Currently, communication between that place and the outside world, telegrams must all pass through Tokyo, and mail must also be subject to strict inspection. For example, the telegram sent from Shenyang on the 25th of last month, the manuscript sent by the correspondent by mail has now been received. After checking, a paragraph has been deleted by the censor, which states that a certain Chinese deputy comprador of Citibank went to the Frontier Bank to collect 400,000 yuan, but was brutally beaten by Japanese soldiers and imprisoned in a room. Finally, he managed to report to the Citibank manager, who reported it to the American consul and protested to the Japanese consul, and was then released. Furthermore, the Frontier Bank was also ordered by the Japanese military authorities not to pay checks issued by the Beiping-Liaoning Railway Bureau for the construction of the Huludao seaport by the Dutch company. Although the Japanese government and the Japanese representative in Geneva have declared that Chinese government-run banks and silver firms have resumed business, Zhuang placed them under strict restrictions. Except for a very small limit on personal accounts, they are practically unable to operate. Recently, the commander of the Kwantung Army issued a notice authorizing soldiers to seal up businesses when they suspect them of trading with the enemy of the Japanese army. In the past, most of the transactions of foreign merchants here were related to Chinese government agencies. The new regulations of the Japanese army have caused business to stagnate. Foreign banks and businesses have been greatly affected. It is reported that American merchants have reported this situation to their headquarters in New York, Chicago, etc., requesting direct intervention from the US State Department, etc. In addition, regarding the news that Han De, the correspondent of the International News Agency, and Professor Thorfrann of the University of California were arrested for taking pictures at Shenyang Station, it was stated that the American consul had lodged a formal protest because the Japanese consul and military authorities had stated that photography was allowed. However, when a representative of Paramount Pictures wanted to film a movie recently, the Japanese banned the filming of newsreels and only allowed them to film some unimportant movies on the streets of the Japanese concession, etc., which was also deleted by the Japanese censor. The harshness of the censorship can be seen from this."

The Japanese Army's Absurd Claims in Andong

▲Regardless of Everything, Moving Forward Bravely▲Not Afraid of Even the Allied Nations

"A correspondent from Andong reports that the Japanese army occupying Andong withdrew a portion of its troops on the 30th of last month. Currently, only the Maritime Public Security Bureau, the Commercial Port Public Security Bureau, the County Public Security Bureau, and the County Government are stationed with Japanese military police. The Japanese troops from other agencies have already been withdrawn. Since the withdrawal of the Japanese army, they have repeatedly posted so-called announcements to reassure the people. Recently, a red paper leaflet printed in lead type was posted in the city, with the title 'Determination of the Japanese Army.' The original text is as follows: 'The occurrence of this major incident in Manchuria is also considered a great regret by us soldiers. However, since the situation is already like this, we must be aware of turning disaster into blessing. We firmly believe that through this incident, we can liberate the 30 million people of the Northeast. From now on, we soldiers will work harder to completely settle the 30 million people of the Northeast in a happy state, until the construction of a civilized paradise for the Japanese, Koreans, Manchus, Mongols, and Chinese masses is completed. The two previous Sino-Japanese and Russo-Japanese wars, plus this incident, are all aimed at establishing the right to self-defense for the survival of the Japanese nation and bringing peace to the East. The mission of us Japanese soldiers is completely upright and great, which is of course understandable to the general public. In order to seek the happiness of the 30 million people of the Northeast and complete this great undertaking, we soldiers realize that it will take two or three years. During the period when we soldiers complete this undertaking, we must be fearless and move forward bravely, brace our spirits, overcome all difficulties, and steadily and step by step open up a paradise with practical achievements, taking this justice as the foundation and spreading the Kingly Way. However, if anyone interferes with us soldiers, no matter who it is, they will all be regarded as enemies and conquered. Even if it is the allied nations, we have nothing to fear.' (November 5th)."

Central Committee and National Government Memorial Week

▲Central Party Headquarters, 9 AM on the 9th, the Central Party Headquarters held the 137th Premier's Memorial Week, attended by Chiang Kai-shek, Zhang Ji, He Yingqin, Zhu Peide, Liu Wendao, Ding Weifen, Zhu Jiahua, Ye Chucang, Cai Yuanpei, Chen Mingshu, Wu Tiecheng, Fang Juehui, Chen Guofu, Chen Lifu, Chen Bulei, Cheng Tianfang, Chu Minyi, Miao Peicheng, Enhebatu, Huang Shi, Kong Xiangxi, Wang Jiuling, Chen Zhaoying, Yu Jingtang, and all the reducers, a total of more than 600 people. After Chairman Chiang Kai-shek led the ceremony, Zhang Ji reported that our country is now facing such a difficult time. During the Premier's Memorial Week, we always feel sorry for the Premier in front of the Premier's portrait. If the Premier were still alive, our country would be very strong, and the current difficulties could also be safely overcome under the leadership of the Premier. Now, unfortunately, the Premier can no longer personally lead us. When we encounter such a national disaster, comrades often think about how to repay the Premier, inherit the Premier's legacy, and follow the Premier's instructions to overcome this difficulty. I personally believe that the Kuomintang has a revolutionary history of more than 40 years, and it was created by the Premier's lifelong hardships. We have this foundation of more than 40 years, relying on the Premier's spirit in heaven, we will be able to unite and save this national disaster. As long as we all have self-confidence and unity, we will be able to repay the people and live up to our ancestors of 4,000 years. But if we want to save the country, we must identify our policies and paths, especially to recognize the general trend in the world. For more than ten years, I have often paid attention to the relationship between China and Japan, and the relationship between the Chinese Kuomintang and Japan. I feel that on the one hand, China and Japan have the same language and culture, and should logically become brotherly countries. On the other hand, the Premier has spent a lot of effort to promote Japan's awareness, and China and Japan should work together to maintain peace in East Asia and promote East Asian civilization. However, the Premier's hard work and efforts have resulted in zero. The fault lies not in China, not in the Chinese Kuomintang, but in Japan, especially the Japanese warlords. Since the Meiji Restoration, Japan has taken the wrong path because of its military victory. The Japanese warlords are very domineering, and Asia has become an unstable situation. In Europe, large and small countries with different languages and cultures can coexist and prosper, but Japan is always destroying international morality, only seeking its own survival and prosperity, regardless of the world's public opinion. On the one hand, it uses force to annex. Ryukyu is a beautiful island, under the protection of China, it was extremely peaceful, but Japan insisted on annexing it. Taiwan followed the same path. Korea has a history of 2,000 years of independence, and China has always recognized its independent status, but Japan also destroyed it. In this case, how can Japan be said to be a civilized country, a country that abides by international morality? This time, the issue of the three northeastern provinces occurred, and Japan took the wrong path again. So Japan's past actions are all wrong, they are the behavior of aggression in the Middle Ages. I often go to Japan and point out their mistakes to the Japanese. From more than ten years of observation, I know that although Japan is not without people who understand the general trend, the awakened elements are ultimately no match for the traditional forces of the Japanese warlords. I often feel that if Japan does not correct its delusional psychology, it will eventually become an obstacle to world peace. This time, the Japanese army invaded and occupied our eastern provinces, which can be regarded as fully demonstrating their tyranny. China has suffered such a major insult. In order to protect the survival of the nation and public opinion, in addition to the determination to die, unite and fight to the end, there is no other way out. From the end of the 18th century to the beginning of the 19th century, Napoleon invaded Germany. After the German people were ravaged by France, what was the attitude of their nation? In 1870, after the Franco-Prussian War, Germany regained the two states of Alsace-Lorraine and besieged Paris, making a city-under-siege alliance. From that time until 1914, during these 44 years, what was the spirit of the French people? Since the Western countries have such good precedents in front of them, we should follow their spirit to deal with the national crisis. China is the most peace-loving nation in the world, and it is also a nation that does not hesitate to sacrifice everything to support public opinion. Therefore, we have no so-called relatives, enemies, friends, or enemies in the world. Any country that can respect public opinion can be regarded as a friendly country. In the past few years, we have made a mistake ourselves, that is, we only shouted to overthrow all imperialism, but we have not been able to work hard, strive for self-reliance, and show the strength of our nation. So the Japanese took this opportunity to think that they could take advantage of the situation, and greatly exerted their strength. Now the International League of Nations and friendly countries have felt that upholding public opinion and protecting world peace is the common responsibility of the world and our China. The world has a full understanding of our spirit of upholding public opinion and resisting violence. We should correct and punish these bad elements and bad nations in the world, which is not worthy of the meaning of the modern world. Our nation must also have its own meaning, to unite and express that 400 million Chinese people are a whole nation, and give play to our strength. But the so-called 400 million people uniting is an empty word. The most important thing is that our Kuomintang, which leads the people, must hold the supreme sacrifice and unite, and then we can lead the people, compete for our position in the world, and get international assistance. Then the unscrupulous country will not be afraid that he will not yield or bow his head. After the report, the meeting adjourned."

The Impasse of the Jiaoji Coal Surge Remains Unresolved

▲Miners and coal merchants will go to Beijing again to petition

"A correspondent from Jinan reports that the miners and coal merchants along the Jiaoji Railway announced a strike on the 1st due to the Jiaoji Railway's increase in freight rates by 20%. As of today (the 7th), it has been a week and has not yet returned to normal. Jinan does not store much coal, and the winter demand is very urgent. The coal source has been cut off for the past 7 days, and the coal price has gradually increased. Although the Ministry of Railways has mediated in the middle, the Railway Bureau and the miners and coal merchants have held meetings in Qingdao, but the meetings have broken down and there is no hope of resolution. Now, the representatives of the miners and coal merchants, Ding Jingchen and others, have arrived in Jinan again. According to the talks, the Railway Bureau initially requested during the Qingdao meeting: (1) The Railway Bureau purchases coal at the old price, paying 4.7 yuan per ton; (2) Coal for domestic sales still increases the freight rate by 20% (the reason is that the coal mining industry has recognized it in April). The miners and coal merchants believe that purchasing coal at the old price of 4.7 yuan per ton is too much of a loss and cannot comply with the order. A lower price is acceptable. The second point is that the increase in freight rates for domestic sales must be completely canceled, because differential treatment cannot face the mainland public. Later, the Railway Bureau stated that the Ministry of Railways could cancel the increase in domestic sales, so it indicated that (1) the Jiaoji Railway could increase the coal purchase price; (2) the increase in domestic sales could be canceled, but the order to cancel the domestic price increase must be issued after the road coal price is stipulated. The miners and coal merchants believe that the stipulation of the road coal price and the cancellation of the domestic sales price increase cannot be confused, and must be handled separately. The Railway Bureau should not use this as a threat, and the meeting became deadlocked. It is reported that Ding Jingchen, Yang Yuan, Li Zumo and others have scheduled to go to Beijing from Jinan on the 8th to petition the Ministry of Railways again. (November 7th)"

On the 8th of this month, the water police encountered bandits in front of the temple and captured a bandit ship. Changshu

"Private Smuggling Squad Destroys Xiaoyao You Theater" After Xu Biyun came to Changshu to perform at the local Xiaoyao You Theater, business was not very prosperous. Because the ticket collection problem was slightly stricter, a plainclothes officer from the tenth private smuggling squad stationed in Changshu had an argument at the theater because he did not buy a ticket. Unexpectedly, the officer harbored resentment and gathered many officers on the night of the 7th, dressed in various clothes, some in plain clothes and some in military uniforms, to watch the play at the theater. Unexpectedly, at about 9 PM, on the pretext of tea, a man blew a police whistle, and they stood up from all sides and started beating people. At that time, teacups, teapots, tables and chairs were flying around, and the order was in chaos. The audience fled in panic, and those who could not escape were also affected. The police officers who were suppressing the scene could not stop them and left. The officers did whatever they wanted. After the theater was destroyed, they went outside to find staff to beat up, and also went to the Yingming Club to destroy it. The glass windows and teacups were broken, and the tables and chairs were also knocked down. At that time, Gao, the company commander of the garrison security team, happened to be present. Seeing this situation, he was furious. Because he had a short gun in the hands of the police, he showed it as a warning. The private smuggling officers then blew the whistle and left. When they left, they also stood in line outside and reported the number, so this matter was definitely prepared in advance. The theater stopped playing that night, and the directors before and after the stage demanded that the garrison police and the Public Security Bureau do their best to protect them. Shen, the battalion commander of the security team, rushed to the scene after hearing the news. The officers who caused the trouble had already dispersed, so he called Wang Zushan, the captain of the squadron, to Jincheng to handle the aftermath. At that time, Wang had just returned from Shanghai and did not know the details. Hearing the alarming news, he put on his clothes and entered the city. At that time, Battalion Commander Shen, for the sake of local security and military discipline, had a negotiation with Wang. Xuan Wang admitted that the restraint was not strong and was willing to take full responsibility. It was not until dawn that the discussion was settled. After Captain Wang Zushan of the private smuggling squad returned to the squadron, he found out that the culprit was Zhuang Keqin, the captain of the No. 1 patrol boat, and immediately sent him to the Public Security Bureau to be dealt with according to law. On the one hand, he also punished the officers who caused the trouble with military sticks, and then entered the city to investigate the theater and was willing to compensate for all losses and apologize to all parties. The Yingming Club, in the inspection of losses, found a box of cannonballs, so they immediately sent representatives to the Public Security Bureau to meet with Director Yin Peng, handed in a memorial, demanding that the troublemakers compensate for the losses, and also asked to investigate the bullets. Xuan Jing, the private smuggling team, declared that the squadron headquarters did not have a short gun, and that no one was carrying a weapon at that time, so the lost bullet was definitely not left by the officers of the team, and also requested an investigation. Therefore, Yin, the director of the Public Security Bureau, must carefully study this bullet and strive to understand it. As for Yang Keqin, the culprit who was taken away, he will either be sent to the judiciary or the camp headquarters for punishment in the future. The theater will still perform as usual the next day.

"The Case of the Sudden Death of a Female Principal Involves Relevant Persons" In the case of Hu Tinglian, the female principal of Yanhang Elementary School, whose death is unknown, the family members have now twisted Wu Xiaosheng, who is a major suspect, to the Public Security Bureau, and transferred him to the judiciary for interrogation. Now, the hearing officer Yang Xin has summoned Wang Yin, a female maid of the school, and Zhang Xiguan, a local Ding, for a secret interrogation, and banned onlookers. The plaintiff Hu Yuanpu (the cousin of the deceased) requested the court to thoroughly investigate the cause of death in detail to clear the injustice. Wu Xiaosheng still confessed that because his son was studying at the school, he had been acting as a doctor and decocting medicine, but he did not know anything else. The local Ding and the female school servant all confessed that they did not know the cause of death. Xuan will temporarily detain Wu, and the school servant will be released by the local Ding for investigation and verification. However, the relatives of the corpse have now found a photo of a man and many love letters in the coffin of the deceased, with the signature Gu Moumou. It is said that Hu Tinglian was quite romantic during her lifetime. When she was the principal of Xieqiao Elementary School, she had a relationship with Gu, which was later discovered. The tabloids detailed the matter, so the authorities dismissed her. Afterwards, there were frequent letters and correspondence. Now, Gu is working in the Third Education Hall and likes painting. The relatives of the corpse also believe that this person has a major relationship, and immediately requested the Education Bureau to thoroughly investigate.

Wuxi

Robbery of Three Families and Assault of Victims in the Sixteenth District (Tianxia City), near the Tangtou Town of Zhuxiang. Yang Genpan, a villager from the countryside, has been a steady farmer. On the evening of the eighth day of the previous month, at 11 PM, seven robbers suddenly appeared, dressed in short blue cloth shirts, wearing peaked caps, speaking in a strong northern accent. Each held a fake handgun, broke down the door, and immediately beat up Yang Genpan's grandmother, Mrs. Hu, severely. Her left shoulder, eyes, ears, and other areas were seriously injured. The robbers then searched the house, stealing over thirty silver dollars from a Buddhist association. Subsequently, they went to Xie Gansheng's house in Xiexing for robbery. When they saw Xie's son, A Da's wife, Mrs. Li, who was heavily pregnant, they became enraged and kicked her twice. Mrs. Li's fetus was seriously injured, and she immediately collapsed on the ground, unconscious. They dragged Gansheng's sick wife from the bed, forcing her to reveal the location of hidden silver. They then ransacked boxes and chests, extensively looting, resulting in a loss of over two hundred dollars. Finally, they went to a certain surname's house in Lixing for robbery, the amount of loss is unknown.

Jiangyin

Factory Cloth Merchants Oppose Changing the Principles of the Fine Yarn Fund. The dyeing and weaving factories in Jiangyin use fine yarn and thread, which are scarce in domestic production, and have been buying Japanese goods. Since the Wanbaoshan Incident in September, the whole country has been indignant and boycotting Japanese goods. The Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association, for the sake of raw materials for various factories, imitated the "May 3rd" anti-Japanese measures and levied a fine yarn factory fund. It was agreed that this fund would be collected up to one million taels, and then action would be taken to open the factory. If the amount was insufficient, the factories in various counties would subscribe for shares. On September 18th, the violent Japanese invaded our three northeastern provinces. The Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association collected the aforementioned fund until September 25th. After that, Japanese yarn was boycotted entirely. However, the fund collected has not yet reached one million taels, and should be retained as planned. Recently, the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association changed the proposal to establish a yarn sizing factory. After the announcement was issued, manufacturers in Su, Chang, Cheng, and Xi unanimously expressed their opposition. The other day, the Dyeing and Weaving Association of the four counties of Cheng, Xi, Wu, and Yu sent a letter to the Jiangyin Factory Cloth Guild, seeking their opinion, and also replied expressing unanimous opposition.

Villagers Falsely Claim to be Zhang Jingjiang's Brother-in-Law. Guo Xingbao, a farmer from the Sanduan Village in Yangku Town, is a Catholic. His younger sister was sold to a Zhang family in Nanxun, Zhejiang Province, as a concubine. Guo deceives the ignorant villagers in the countryside, falsely claiming that Zhang Jingjiang, an important figure in the Party and the state, is his sister's husband. Ignorant villagers believe it to be true. Recently, he illegally gathered a society and named it "Yitou." Yesterday (the 7th), Guo Shengxing, a member of the Education Association of the village, and Xu Dianren, a member of the Education Association, jointly reported to the county. Guo was arrested and brought to the county, where Magistrate Ma personally interrogated him. Guo strongly argued that the allegations were all false accusations driven by personal grudges. The court ordered him to be released on bail.

Zhenjiang

Meeting to Discuss the Silk Reeling Industry Labor Dispute. Workers from the Zhenjiang silk reeling industry union, because the factory had received debt maintenance funds but delayed the start of work, cutting off the workers' livelihoods, gathered at the Chamber of Commerce the other day to petition, requesting that a way be found to maintain their jobs, and refused to disperse. The Shanghai Public Security Bureau Inspector Xu persuaded them and promised to find a solution, and they dispersed. It is reported that the Public Security Bureau has sent letters to the County Party Department, the County Government, and the Silk Reeling Industry Union to hold a meeting today to discuss everything.

Forgery of Recommendation Letter Leads to Court Investigation. Since the news of the dismissal of Li Zonggang, the chief of the Public Security Bureau of Wujin County, spread, those waiting for appointment were eager to get the position. Chen Xiaowu, a Guangdong native who had previously passed the qualification examination with the eleventh rank, had the audacity to forge a recommendation letter from Lei Xiaocen, an advisor to the Ministry of Interior, and presented it to Director Hu of the Civil Affairs Department, requesting to be immediately appointed as the chief of the Public Security Bureau of Wujin County. Later, Hu replied to Advisor Lei, saying that the chief of the Public Security Bureau of Wujin County had already been transferred from Fang Weizhou, the chief of the Public Security Bureau of Taicang County, which was contrary to Lei's intention, hoping to be forgiven. Lei was deeply surprised after receiving the letter and immediately wrote to Director Hu, stating that he had never issued a letter of introduction, asking him to pay attention. Unexpectedly, Chen suddenly brought a second letter in the name of Lei Xiaocen to the department, the content of which was to ask to find a way to arrange an early appointment. In order to be cautious, Director Hu sent Inspector Lu Yonghuang to visit Lei in Beijing with Chen's letter. After verification, it was proven that Chen had indeed borrowed a name and forged a private seal. Lu immediately returned and reported. Director Hu then issued a handwritten order yesterday to Shen Jianhao, the commander of the Special Service Battalion of the Security Department, to arrest Chen at his address and temporarily hand him over to the guard for custody. At the same time, he prepared an official letter, along with the evidence, and escorted him to the Zhenjiang Local Court for detention and investigation.

Magistrate of Taicang County Accused. The Jiangsu Provincial Government has previously received a report from Yang Gang and others, the director of the slaughter tax office in Taicang County, accusing Wu Deyao, the magistrate of the county, of abusing his power due to personal grudges, unlawfully arresting people, and acting illegally. They requested that he be handed over to the court for punishment according to the law. They also accused Shen Yan, the director of the Education Bureau of the county, of deliberately trying to evade responsibility and fleeing his post, requesting that the county be ordered to detain him pending judicial trial, in order to warn officials against evil and avoid injustice. After reviewing the case, the Provincial Government considered that the case was of great importance and had yesterday consulted the Jiangsu High Court for verification.

Sanke Tree Town Robbed by Bandits. Sanke Tree Town, forty miles away from Huaiyin County, is near Siyang and is often disturbed by bandits. Ministry of Education Cables to Retain Zhejiang University President Shao

▲Shao Cables Again Requesting Resignation

Zhejiang University experienced a disturbance on the 4th of this month. President Shao Feizi telegraphed the Ministry of Education that evening to resign from his post. This was reported in this newspaper. We now know that the Ministry of Education replied on the 6th, urging him to overcome the difficulties and not consider resigning, and to investigate and punish the students who caused the trouble. However, Shao's determination to resign is firm. Yesterday, he telegraphed the Ministry of Education again to resign. The telegram is recorded as follows:

▲Ministry of Education's telegram to Shao, President of Zhejiang University: Received your telegram. The students who caused the trouble on that day should be investigated and punished as soon as possible. The affairs of Zhejiang University are important. It is hoped that you will overcome the difficulties and not consider resigning. Ministry of Education [seal].

▲Shao Feizi's telegram to the Ministry of Education in Nanjing: Received your telegram, instructing me to continue in my position and to investigate and punish the students who caused the trouble. I should comply with your instructions. However, I am of low ability and cannot fulfill the Ministry's intention to rectify the academic atmosphere. Previously, Dean Li of the College of Engineering submitted his resignation, taking responsibility for inadequate management and training. The original submission was returned. Regarding the reasons for the telegram, in addition to being copied and sent to the various colleges by the Secretariat, I earnestly request that my resignation be approved immediately and that someone be selected to take over as soon as possible. Shao Feizi presents respectfully.

Zhejiang Education Department Orders Counties and Cities to Abolish Two Types of Education Committees

The Zhejiang Education Department previously resolved to abolish various education committees in counties and cities in the province at the Provincial Local Education Administration Conference. After investigation, there are currently seven types of education committees established in various counties and cities in the province: (1) County and City Education Committees, (2) County and City Education Property Management Committees, (3) County and City Compulsory Education Committees, (4) County and City Mass Education Committees, (5) County and City Literacy Campaign Promotion Committees, (6) Phonetic Symbol Promotion Committees, and (7) County and City Education Economic Audit Committees. After further review, it was decided that: A. Since the County and City Education Committees are responsible for reviewing the guidelines and plans for education in the counties and cities, all matters related to mass education and compulsory education can be reviewed by this committee. B. The Literacy Campaign Promotion Committees and the Phonetic Symbol Promotion Committees are temporary in nature. The latter should be abolished, and the County Education Bureaus and City Education Sections should be responsible for handling their affairs. C. The County Education Property Management Committees and the County and City Education Economic Audit Committees should remain as they are. A special document was prepared to be submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval. The Ministry of Education has now approved, stating that the Phonetic Symbol Promotion Committees have already been ordered to be followed by all provinces and cities and should not be abolished alone. The rest are approved as proposed. An order was issued to all counties yesterday to comply with this.

Education Department Approves Jiangyin's Educational Budget for the Twentieth Year

The Jiangsu Education Department reviewed Jiangyin County Government's revised educational budget for the 20th year of the Republic, finding that the revised plan generally conformed with requirements. New projects such as adding schools and classrooms should be reported separately with detailed information. The simplified primary schools to be established in the compulsory education experimental zone require detailed plans and expenditure breakdowns to be reported for approval. Before approval is obtained, no expenditures may be made without authorization. A special order was given to the county government to implement the plan as proposed, and to forward the order for compliance. A preliminary disbursement book, Compulsory Education No. 1, for 28,000 yuan, and a People's Education No. 1 disbursement book for 12,000 yuan, are approved. The remaining amount will be applied for after the start of the second semester.

French Lawn Tennis Association Officially Announces World's Top Ten Tennis Players

Paris, 10th - The French Lawn Tennis Association officially announced today in the Paris newspapers the top ten tennis players in the world. Cochet remains in first place, and the 19-year-old American Vines is second. In total, the United States occupies five spots, England and France two each, and Japan one. The list is as follows:

1st Cochet (France) 2nd Vines (USA)

3rd Perry (England) 4th Austin (England)

5th Shields (USA) 6th Wood (USA)

7th Borotra (France) 8th Jiro Sato (Japan)

9th Van Ryn (USA) 10th Lott (USA)

Below them are Menzel (Czechoslovakia), Boussus (France), Doeg (USA), Hughes (England), and Tilden (Italy).

▲The ranking, with Vines listed in second place, is largely due to his special performance in the U.S. Open. Although Vines did not participate in this year's Wimbledon and Davis Cup, opinions differ on Perry and Austin above Shields and Wood. This can be explained as follows: Although Shields and Wood won the Wimbledon finals, Shields completely lost his form in the England-America Davis Cup inter-zone final in Paris. Although he beat Perry, he ultimately lost to Austin. Although Wood defeated Perry and Hughes at Wimbledon, he lost both matches in the Davis Cup inter-zone final, once to Austin and again to Perry. He also lost to Perry in Newport. Borotra's decline this season is undeniable, but he is still a formidable force in indoor matches, so he remains in the top ten.
