Free Talk

Memories of a Tortoiseshell Beam

— Swallow

▲The Heroic Death of Zuo Baogui

In the Battle of Pyongyang, Zuo Baogui defended the West Gate alone with one army against the enemy's entire division. (Zuo, as a registered admiral with a yellow riding jacket, double-eyed peacock feather, and double-numbered Baturu title, was subordinate to Ye Zhichao). At that time, Wei Rugui fled first, and Ye also fled after. Nie Gongting fought and retreated, losing only a limited amount. When Zuo heard of this, his hair stood on end and split. He waved a red flag and personally supervised the battle. Japanese troops attacked from all sides, and bullets rained down. Zuo's double-eyed peacock feather was burned by artillery shells, leaving only the feather shaft, which was still burning as he fired on the enemy, killing hundreds of Japanese soldiers. After a day and night of bitter fighting, more than half of his troops were lost. A certain officer tried to persuade Zuo to retreat to plan for another attempt. Zuo drew his saber, cut a piece of his clothing hem, and told the crowd, "Today's matter, anyone who retreats will be like this hem." Looking back at his subordinates, only three hundred or so people remained, and an enemy bullet flew and hit his left arm. Zuo did not move, suppressed the wound, and fought again. He took the lead, killing dozens of Japanese chiefs with his bare hands. The enemy troops gathered more and more, and Zuo glared and shouted, charging into the battle and being struck by bullets in the abdomen and back. His horse died, and Zuo also fell. Under the anger of his subordinates, each fought as if they were a hundred men. When the ammunition ran out, the entire army was wiped out. Only four or five people escaped back, recounting the tragic scene of his death. Everyone who heard it could not help but shed tears. He can be compared to Deng Shichang of the Navy, who died one after the other. Alas.

Don't Remove the Weeds in the Courtyard - A Collection of Husband's Talks

At the Lunch Table

Do you study Buddhism? Why don't you eat meat?

I have no inventions, cannot work, and make no contribution to society. I am already ashamed to be a parasite. If I were to eat meat, harm their lives, and support this useless person, that would be even more unthinkable.

According to what you say, none of us should eat meat. Who has inventions? Who can work? Who deserves beef?

Correct! All of us useless eaters should simply be vegetarians. Perhaps only Auntie Min, who carries water and cooks, deserves to eat meat!

Good! Let's give all the meat dishes to Auntie Min to eat!

Does Auntie Jin, who carries the child, deserve to eat meat? Since Auntie Min has meat to eat, it seems unfair to be partial.

That depends on who Auntie Jin is carrying the child for. If the child's mother is a worker in a scientific laboratory or a female worker in a yarn factory, then Auntie Jin is helping someone invent or work, and she deserves our gifts. If the child's mother hires Auntie Jin to carry the child so that she can go out to play cards or be comfortable at home, then Auntie Jin is a helper, not a helper, and she is not worthy of eating meat like us.

You say that laborers deserve to eat meat, but in this unequal society, laborers cannot afford to buy meat dishes.

As long as the elite idlers, scholars, masters, wives, young ladies, hooligans, and all those who cannot invent and cannot work are only allowed to be vegetarians, then they will naturally have meat to eat.

This is not thorough enough! Invention and labor are individual contributions to humanity. What does that have to do with animals? It is not necessarily fair to take the lives of cows, sheep, pigs, chickens, ducks, and fish to repay their merits.

Good, let's all be vegetarians!

The Enemy Tower for Defending Against the Japanese Pirates in Pingwang

— Zheng Yimei

Pingwang is a small town belonging to Wujiang County, about forty-odd li from the city. Yingdu Lake nearby is especially a famous scenic area. In the past, when I bought a boat to tour Yuhang, I passed by here at dusk. The misty smoke and water made it difficult to distinguish. A few years ago, I went to Lihuali for business. On the way back, I went from Lihuali to Pingwang, and then from Pingwang I took a ferry to Jiahe. Lihuali is only twelve li away from Pingwang by water. While waiting for the boat, I stayed on the wharf for about an hour, allowing me to appreciate the scenery of the place. The market street is extremely short, and the residents are mostly simple and unadorned. However, there are many monasteries, and the prevalence of superstition is remarkable here. Because it is near the water, it is rich in fish, shrimp, water chestnuts, and gorgon fruits. I also heard that there is a kind of red shrimp produced under a certain bridge, with red body and dragon-like whiskers, different from ordinary ones. It is said that crossing the bridge will not find it. It is said that immortals cooked shrimp with wine, became drunk, and spat under the bridge, which then turned into a different species. This is a preposterous talk and not credible. During the Jiajing period of the Ming Dynasty, Japanese pirates invaded our borders. Yang Zhi, a local official, was worried about it. He gathered workers to build an enemy tower north of the Elder Bridge. When the pirates disturbed Pingwang, Yang Zhi personally led local soldiers and civilians to defend it from the enemy tower. Arrows and stones rained down, and the Japanese general Matsumura Yoshishi was killed. The remaining pirates retreated down the boats, raised their sails, and fled. Yang Zhi pursued them and overturned countless boats. The spirit of the Japanese pirates was greatly frustrated. As times changed, the enemy tower gradually collapsed. Today, only a few zhang of stone foundation remain. Copper camels and brambles make one feel sentimental without even visiting the Luoyang Palace Gate.

World Short Chronicle

— Haike

The First Automobile. The history of the automobile is almost a century old. Recently, Austria held a centennial celebration for the creator of the first automobile. This creator was named Siegfried Marcus. People in Central Europe generally say that he was truly the first contributor to the creation of the automobile. His first automobile was created in 1864. At that time, it used oil. In the early stages of its creation, of course, there were many imperfections. He put in a lot of research and greatly improved it, and in 1875 he created a better automobile. This car is still preserved in the capital city of Vienna for observation. However, Marcus's car was lacking in many mechanical aspects and could not propel itself. One hundred and twenty-eight years ago, an English inventor, R. Trevithick, created a steam car and drove it through the streets of London. For a long time, this steam car was very popular and competed fiercely with trains. Automobiles can now be seen almost everywhere in the modern world, but to trace its origins, one must give credit to Marcus and Trevithick.

Recent News of Wu Peifu

— Bing Ding

General Wu Ziyu, who dreamed of unifying the country by force, suffered a setback at Yuguan and a second defeat at Wuhan. He has been living in seclusion in Sichuan for several years, under the protection of Sichuan generals Yang Sen and Deng Xihou, and has long been forgotten by the world. Recently, with the rampant violence of the Japanese, seizing our Northeast, killing our compatriots, and destroying our construction, all those with a little hot blood are filled with indignation. Therefore, there is an urgent need to plan for national unity to jointly resist foreign aggression, and to concentrate diplomatic and military talents to work together to save the country from the storms. Thus, there is a rumor that Wu is being brought back into service. However, the roads are far, and news of Wu is occasionally found in the newspapers, but ultimately, the details cannot be known. Yesterday, a guest came from Shaanxi. Shaanxi and Sichuan are close neighbors. He spoke very detailedly about Wu's situation, saying that Wu had been in seclusion in Sichuan for a long time, and his ambition had never ceased for a day, only that the time had not come. In August, there was a coup in Gansu. Chairman Ma Hongbin was detained by Lei Zhongtian and Ma Wenche. The political power in Gansu was concentrated in the hands of Lei and Ma. Lei then sent troops to attack Ma Tingxian's troops in Longnan, hoping to confiscate Ma's weapons to strengthen his forces. Ma was no match and retreated, gathering on the Sichuan border. Knowing that Wu's reputation was very prominent, he wanted to gather Wu to rally support. He sent an envoy to welcome Wu. Wu thought that this was the opportunity to mediate the Gansu situation and went to Wudu in the name of Commander-in-Chief of the Anguo Army to mediate the dispute between Ma and Lei. On one hand, he united Deng Xihou and Yang Sen in Sichuan as a backing. However, among the Gansu generals, in addition to Lei Zhongtian, there were also Lu Dachang and Chen Zhanggui, two divisions with strong forces, who obeyed Yang Hucheng, the director of the Northwest Appeasement Headquarters. Lei did not dare to openly oppose the Central Government because Lu and Chen sincerely obeyed Yang. Wu had not received an order from the Central Government, so he could not be considered official. Lu and Chen rejected Wu's envoy without comment. Thus, Wu could not immediately go to Lanzhou and only ordered Bai Jianwu to persuade Ma Lin of Qinghai and Lei, Lu, and Chen not to meet each other with force and to seek compromise conditions. However, no substantial progress has been made to date. Therefore, Wu is only staying in Wudu and has not entered Lanzhou. Wu's subordinates have been scattered. Those who went to Wudu this time were only the guards led by Bai Jianwu, more than 600 people. These 600-odd people have never left Wu since Wu entered Sichuan, because they share the same joys and sorrows with Wu.

The Necessary Understanding of Resisting Japan and Saving the Nation

— En Pu

(1) Resisting Japan and saving the nation is a painstaking and arduous task. It is definitely not a fashionable act.

(2) Resisting Japan and saving the nation is a righteous and urgent act of self-defense. It is definitely not an anti-foreign, quarrelsome, sneaky, and petty act.

(3) Resisting Japan and saving the nation is my personal duty. I should lead by example and be a guide for others.

(4) Persuading people to resist Japan and save the nation is my personal responsibility. If people do not listen, it is their fault. I must not stop my work of persuasion because people do not listen.

(5) If people do not resist Japan and save the nation, it is their sin. Since I recognize resisting Japan and saving the nation as a legitimate act, I must not be discouraged or stop my work because of their sins.

(6) Teaching others how to resist Japan and save the nation is the highest public virtue, a benevolent act of saving people from fire and water.

(7) Asking people to teach me how to resist Japan and save the nation is a clever plan to gather wisdom and benefit. It is the best way to avenge and redress grievances, and it is definitely not an expression that I am inferior to others and willingly show weakness.

(8) Resisting Japan and saving the nation by outwardly complying but inwardly opposing is a suicidal policy and a great farce that makes foreign countries laugh.

(9) Resisting Japan and saving the nation requires long-term and patient perseverance. Five minutes of enthusiasm is in vain.

(10) Resisting Japan and saving the nation requires a spirit of great fearlessness. No external force can overwhelm my inner resistance to Japan and saving the nation.

(11) Boycotting Japanese goods and not cooperating with them is the most peaceful, easiest, and most effective way to resist Japan and save the nation.

(12) Implementing a conscription system to strengthen the physique and implementing compulsory vocational education to popularize mass education are the supreme national salvation policies.

My Business Talk (Part 1)

— Tianxu Wosheng

In the past two months, entrepreneurs who want to save the country and seek to benefit both themselves and others have asked me to plan and design for them. It can be said to be extremely prosperous for a while. However, I believe that no matter what kind of business, if its capital is limited, it will often run out of steam halfway and fall down. It is very dangerous. For example, it is not difficult to make a small industrial product with a capital of several thousand. However, to sell it in the market, there are three key elements. First, buyers should be able to buy it cheaply and everywhere. Then, it must be widely distributed. If each distributor is given an account of 50 yuan and the cost is 70 percent, then at least 100 companies will need 3,500 yuan. Second, buyers need to know where the goods are sold, which requires advertising. Assuming 20 short lines, each line costing 4.5 jiao, it will cost 9 yuan a day. Publishing in the Shen and Xin newspapers every other day will cost a monthly fee of 270 yuan. At least 500 yuan must be prepared. Third, if the inventory and raw materials are insufficient, then the supply will not meet the demand, which is a major blow. It is like a war, and if the bullets are insufficient, then you cannot advance to attack or retreat to defend, and defeat is inevitable. Therefore, if there are 5,000 yuan of goods in the account, 5,000 yuan of raw materials must be prepared to meet immediate needs, so that they can be turned around and circulated without missing the opportunity. As mentioned above, the fund must be at least 10,000 yuan. The advertising fee is taken from 5 percent of the selling price, which means that at least 10,000 yuan of goods must be sold per month. With a capital of 10,000 yuan, to do 120,000 yuan of business a year, unless it is a store that sells, greets guests at the front door, and receives goods at the back door, those who are good at long-sleeved dancing may still be possible. If it is called a factory, then it is absolutely impossible. The capital of a factory is at least three times: one in the account, one in hand, and one in the warehouse and on the way. Therefore, with a capital of 10,000 yuan, it can only do 20,000 yuan of business a year. At a profit of 30 percent, it is only 6,000 yuan. With 3,000 yuan for advertising, only 3,000 yuan is left. Whether it is enough to cover the expenses, it is not necessary to consult the divination to know. Therefore, I am willing to offer a word of advice based on the principle of being loyal to those who seek advice. Those who want to start a small industry with thousands of gold are better off forming a company and becoming shareholders than doing a one-man show and being stretched everywhere. It is more stable. For example, if you organize a company of 100,000 yuan, the budget is still as above, then you can get thousands of distributors, and you can prepare the needs of thousands of families for inventory and raw materials. But the advertising cost is still only 3,000. With 1,000 distributors, the sales will definitely be ten times wider, and the productivity will also increase ten times.

Rotary Club Novel

A Villager Arrives in Shanghai Again (12)

— Bao Tianxiao

At that time, the villagers, along with the passengers in the third-class car, squeezed out of the small train door like a tide. Although he strongly argued that the military band was welcoming the bride, he actually knew that it must be coming to welcome some rich people. He thought to himself: being rich is really prestigious. Even that group of friends who were eating wedding feasts – whom they called the army – had a decent enough pose.

He didn't bother to investigate whether the soldiers were there to pick up the rice planting committee or the vegetable picking staff. He stumbled out of the train station, first needing to set a direction. Where to go now?

He had a nephew who had a job in Shanghai. That nephew's surname was Lin, and everyone called him Amu Lin. This was teased out by many friends. It is easiest to give people nicknames in Shanghai. It's really one spreads to ten, ten spreads to a hundred. You call, I call, and later it makes it impossible for the person himself to deny it. In fact, it is not surprising that Shanghai addresses people with the word "A". Things like Brother Ade, Brother A Lin, Li Agui, Zhang Agen, and the like are also commonly seen.

"Uncle! It's good that you came to Shanghai to find me, and you can just stay at my place. It doesn't matter." His nephew had said those words to him when he went to the countryside.

"I don't recognize your place, those newly emerging roads in Shanghai, twisting tongues, are hard to remember. What oiled cloth road, wet shirt road, and also Malandang road, more troublesome than reading foreign books." The villager said so.

"The place I live in is easiest to remember. There is a singer named Mei Lanfang, you always know him, right?"

"How could I not know! Even a three-year-old child knows him. I've even seen his photos." The villager again pretended to be an old hand.

"Then I'll tell you! The place I live in is called Meilanfang. The lane houses in Shanghai are all what fang, what li. Meilanfang and Mei Lanfang have the same sound, but the word fang and the word fang are written differently. But when you get to the French Concession, it's easier to ask for Meilanfang. To be honest, I was originally assigned to watch the lane in Fuzhifang. When Fuzhifang is mentioned, some people don't know it very well, but Meilanfang is easier to remember."

"You don't need to remind me, I know all about Mei Lanfang, he is now asking someone to be a matchmaker."

"How do you ask someone to be a matchmaker? I don't know."

"That's right, he has already given his eight characters."

"Haha! I'm afraid you're wrong again, old man. He recently got a doctorate, not gave his eight characters."

Commercial News

Financial - Gold Price Plunges Unceasingly

▲ Further Devastating Drop of 27.4 Taels

Yesterday's gold auction witnessed a horrifying crash approaching 600 taels, with the market in an extremely chaotic state, changing in an instant. The tempestuous volatility caused panic among dealers, with fluctuations of five or six taels occurring frequently. The overall market saw a difference of twenty-four taels. Ultimately, the price plummeted by as much as twenty-seven or twenty-eight taels. This was due to the divergent trend in the silver market and, more significantly, to news that the League of Nations would impose severe sanctions on Japan. The League was reportedly determined to invoke Article 15 of the Covenant and the Kellogg-Briand Pact, considering recalling its ambassador to Japan and imposing an economic blockade. Consequently, many long positions and arbitrageurs had no choice but to sell off in order to prevent further declines and potentially unmanageable losses, especially given the substantial advances extended. As a result, the market opened already below 630 taels, with the downward trend intensifying thereafter. The abnormal weakness of foreign exchange also benefited short sellers, who actively covered their positions. The market price hovered around 610 taels, with the outlook even more frightening. Rumors of a tense situation in Tianjin circulated, along with speculation that the Japanese might withdraw from the League of Nations, further depressing market sentiment. The increasingly loose exchange rate created a sense of being besieged on all sides ("songs of Chu on four sides"), causing a sudden drop to a new low below 605 taels. Further short selling by major players then pushed the price below that level by more than ten taels.

▲ Morning Market Already in a Precarious Situation. The market opened 16.4 mace lower at 624 taels (private deals had gone as low as 30 taels). The Dalian group was the first to sell. The large silver firms reported that the silver telegrams from the previous day had fallen by 16.5 points, but silver prices had risen by 8.3 points. Due to the unfavorable situation, this escalated to 28 taels. In an instant, Zhi Feng, Yong Yuan Mao, Yong Yuan Cheng, Yong Tong, Tai Chang, Zhen Chang Xiang, and others dumped their holdings, causing a further drop to 10.3 mace. Shortly after, it rose to 17 taels as Da De Cheng, Yu Da, and others covered their positions. However, the situation remained unfavorable, leading to another downturn to 11.5 taels. Simultaneously, the foreign exchange market hardened. Banks were buying near-term U.S. dollars at 35.5 yuan and far-term dollars at 35.875 to 35.9375. When British gold was quoted, it rose to 17 taels but remained unchanged. The U.S. dollar was extended by .25, then returned to 16 taels, a rapid increase of 18.5 taels. The cashiers of different firms moved in different directions. At 9:45 a.m., there were fluctuations of two or three taels. HSBC offered one-month British gold at 10 5/8 pence. Ying Tong entered two-month gold at the same price. Subsequently, Zhi Feng, Yong Da Xing, Yong Yuan Cheng, Fu Chang Shun Li, Wan Xing, and arbitrageurs in the U.S. dollar market heavily sold off, causing the price to plummet by 10 taels, reaching 608.5 taels at 10:15 a.m. Later, McGalliard absorbed two-month British gold at .625, and HSBC absorbed three-month U.S. dollars at 36.125 yuan, as well as near-term gold at 36 yuan. Da De Cheng, Heng Xing, Yi Feng, Yong Yuan Mao, Yong Heng Chang Yong, and others successively bought in, pushing the price up by six or seven taels, reaching 15 taels at 10:45 a.m. Afterward, the selling pressure continued, and the price fell again to 608.5 taels. After 11:15 a.m., the market became unpredictable, with fluctuations of four or five taels in an instant, reaching 16 taels by 11:30 a.m. Retail investors chased the price upwards, then weakened. The Indian exchange rate reported a large drop of one rupee and two annas, so the noon close was 12 taels, again reaching 10 taels, and finally 13 or 14 taels. People were extremely confused, and the listed price was changed to 609.67 taels, with an estimated squeeze of around 80 taels.

▲ Besieged on All Sides in the Afternoon. The afternoon market opened weakly at 609 taels, then 612 taels. The Dalian group and Yuan Mao, Yi Feng, and others vigorously sold off. Reports that the riots in Tianjin were becoming more severe circulated, along with rumors that the "dwarf bandits" (Japanese) would withdraw from the League of Nations, causing panic and a drop of 8 taels, ultimately reaching a new low of 604 taels. British gold lengthened to 10 3/4 pence. Before long, Heng Xing, Zhi Feng, Yong and speculators entered the market, causing an upward trend. From 2:10 p.m. to 2:30 p.m., there were fluctuations of four or five taels. Afterwards, Fu Chang, Yuan Heng Shun Li, Da De Cheng, and others took advantage of this to buy in, jumping ten taels, but the foreign exchange market remained flat. At 3:15 p.m., it was 14.8 taels. Subsequently, Da De Cheng, Yi Feng, Zhi Feng, Yong Fu Chang, and others all sold, but it still could not be sustained, and dropped by eight or nine taels, reaching 606 taels at 3:50 p.m. Later, because HSBC and Da Tong were trading one-month U.S. dollars at 36.1875, Zhi Feng, Yong, and retail investors came in again, so at 4:15 p.m., it was 13.5 taels, but retreated to 11 taels shortly after. The Dalian group also sold. By the time the market closed at 4:30 p.m., it had risen again to 13 taels, a devastating drop of 27.4 taels compared to last week. After the market closed, it was re-traded at 11 or 12 taels. Goods and others came out. According to statistics, the largest fluctuation of the day was 28 taels, and the smallest was 604 taels, a difference of 24 taels. The price of goods in the early market was 26.5 taels, the noon close was 12.5 taels, the afternoon was 608.5 taels, and the closing price was 611.5 taels. The quoted price was estimated to be between 90 taels and 83 or 84 taels, with an overnight interest payment of 12 taels and an afternoon interest payment of 13 taels, adding 9 taels to the "red tape" (brokerage fees).

▲ Extremely Complex Speculation. The trading on the table was complex. According to statistics, Yuan Mao Yong, Yi Feng Yong, Heng Xing, Yi Feng, Yu Da, Heng Chang Yong, Fu Tai Heng, Bing Xing, and retail short sellers all bought in. Shun Li, Wan Xing, Da De Cheng, Tong Tai Chang, Zhi Feng Yong, Qian Chang Xiang, Fu Chang, Zhen Chang Xiang, Heng Yu, Ju Chang, Sen Chang Yong, Yuan Cheng Yong, Cui Chang Yong, Yuan Cheng all sold. Wan Xing, Shun Li, Yuan Mao Yong, Yi Feng, Fu Tai Heng, and Heng Chang Yong all sold. Flour Price Plunges Four or Five Fen

Yesterday's flour market unanimously presented a plunging phenomenon. The quoted price of foreign wheat also saw a slight decrease, and the most powerful factor was the sharp fall in the gold price. The high price of the previous month was based on the skyrocketing price of foreign wheat. The current gold price has fallen by about 100 taels compared to that time. The lengthened exchange rate is also a fact that must be reached. If this is reversed, it is no different from the fact that foreign wheat can still be priced. Moreover, the market also rumored that a certain factory had already ordered two ships, and the price was kept secret. In addition, the riots of Japanese wave people in Tianjin also brought about obstacles to future sales. Therefore, from the opening to the closing, people's hearts were unstable from beginning to end, and the prices continued to fall miserably. Observing the subsequent steps, it seems that there are more ominous signs than auspicious signs. As a result, the price for this month plummeted by 4.5 fen compared to the closing price of the previous week, December fell by 5 fen, January fell by 3.75 li, February fell by 3.5 fen, and March and April fell by 2.75 li.

Wheat: Sky-High Dumping

Yesterday, the futures wheat market saw a sharp drop. The quoted price of foreign wheat also fell slightly, and the opening price of the gold market also fell by 20 to 30 taels. The foreign exchange rate was also lengthening step by step. People's hearts were unusually weak. In general, people were afraid of the lengthening of the exchange rate and that foreign wheat would have to come again. Therefore, the major long positions and temporary sky-high positions dumped heavily. The market atmosphere was seen to be collapsing. It is estimated that the recent period fell by 0.78 fen, and the long-term period fell by 0.56 fen. However, in the middle of the day, there were rumors that the United Kingdom purchased a large amount of wheat from the Americas, or that foreign wheat had to re-enter the rising path. People's hearts were stimulated, and the recent period rose by 0.56 fen. As a result, this month fell by 5 fen compared to the previous week, December fell by 5 fen, January fell by 6 fen, February fell by 5 fen, March fell by 4 fen,

Local News

Japanese Army Forcibly Seizes Northeast Salt Tax Case

▲Co-Director Goffe files three reports ▲Japanese army seizes over a million twice ▲Song Ziwen to cable Shi Zhaoji today

Since the incident of the Japanese army forcibly seizing salt tax from the Yingkou and Changchun Salt Revenue Audit Sub-Offices in the three northeastern provinces, the Salt Revenue Audit Office has continuously received telegrams from Mr. Pearson, the director of the Yingkou Sub-Office. The most recent telegram arrived at 5:30 PM yesterday at the local General Office. It has been learned that the Japanese military authorities have forcibly seized the Northeast salt tax twice. The first time was on October 30, when they took 672,000 yuan of salt tax from the Liaoning province from the Yingkou Sub-Office. The second time was on November 6, when they took 720,000 yuan of salt tax from the Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces from the Changchun Sub-Office. The Japanese military authorities also declared that they would extract 45,000 yuan daily.

▲Remarks by Co-Director Goffe A reporter from this newspaper visited Dr. Goffe, Co-Director of the Salt Revenue Audit Office, yesterday. According to him, the fact that the Japanese army has seized the Northeast tax has been successively reported to Finance Minister Song Ziwen and Salt Affairs Director Zhu Tingqi. The Northeast tax collection agencies belong to the central government. Now, the Japanese military authorities are interfering with the tax collection agencies of the internationally recognized National Government by force and forcibly taking the tax, which is an act of violating international law. As for the Japanese representative Yoshizawa, in response to the Chairman of the League of Nations Council Briand regarding this matter, he strongly denied that the Japanese military and police detained the Northeast salt tax and attached a telegram from the Japanese government explaining the truth of the matter, stating that "the Shenyang Local Maintenance Committee requested the transfer of salt surplus from the Yingkou Salt Revenue Audit Sub-Office on September 22, and the audit office personnel replied to the committee, expressing their promise." Dr. Goffe clarified this, saying that after the Japanese army occupied Shenyang at midnight on September 18, they sent personnel to Yingkou and Changchun on the 19th to monitor the Salt Revenue Audit Office, accumulating the daily tax revenue without allowing it to be remitted to the National Government, and only recently took the cash. The date of the incident was actually before the establishment of the Shenyang Local Maintenance Committee.

▲Song Ziwen cables Shi Zhaoji Co-Director Goffe, based on a telegram from Pearson, the director of the Yingkou Sub-Office, has reported twice to Finance Minister Song. Finance Minister Song has also cabled Minister Shi Zhaoji in Geneva to inform the League of Nations Council. Another detailed telegram was originally scheduled to be sent to Geneva last night, but the Salt Affairs General Office received another telegram from the Yingkou Sub-Office at 5:30 PM yesterday. Co-Director Goffe immediately prepared another detailed report last night, requesting Finance Minister Song to, based on the facts, cable Minister Shi to submit it to the League of Nations. Therefore, the Finance Ministry's detailed telegram to Shi needs to be drafted separately and is expected to be sent to Geneva around today or tomorrow.

▲Instructions from the Salt Revenue Audit Office The Salt Revenue Audit Office believes that the Japanese army's forcible seizure of the Northeast salt tax affects the foreign debt guarantee and makes the 1929 foreign debt reorganization plan impossible to implement. Therefore, since this incident occurred, on one hand, it has requested Representative Shi to protest to the League of Nations and demand that Japan return the tax revenue. On the other hand, it has instructed the directors of the Yingkou and Changchun Sub-Offices to protest to the relevant authorities and not to negotiate with any party to avoid misunderstandings. It should be instructed to remit the tax revenue to the National Government as soon as possible. If forcibly obstructed, a protest should be filed. As for the tax revenue arrangements between the central government and Deputy Commander Zhang and other officials, it is an internal matter and cannot be used as an excuse. Chinese and foreign officials of the Salt Revenue Audit Office are not allowed to leave their posts without orders. As for the local situation, Co-Director Goffe personally notified the Japanese Minister Koki Shigemitsu yesterday. Pearson, the director of the Yingkou Sub-Office, telegraphed last night, requesting permission to come to Shanghai to discuss countermeasures.

▲Memorials from the Salt Revenue Audit Office Memorials from Goffe, Co-Director of the Salt Revenue Audit Office, to Song Ziwen, Minister of Finance: (1) (Omitted above) On September 19, the Manchurian Japanese army forcibly occupied the Niuzhuang Salt Revenue Audit Office. Twenty armed soldiers threatened the audit office officials with guns, ordering them not to move. The three guards of the audit office were disarmed, and armed Japanese soldiers were sent to guard the door. All the account books in the office were seized, and another accountant was appointed. The bank that collected taxes on behalf was also occupied. Since then, all tax revenues have been monitored and are not allowed to be remitted to the National Government. (Omitted in the middle) At 10:00 AM on October 31, the director of the Niuzhuang Audit Office telegraphed the following report: On October 30 at 8:00 AM, the Yingkou branch of the Bank of China sent a letter stating that at 11:00 AM today, Yamada, a consultant to the Dongsansheng Guanyin Bank and the Liaoning Provincial Department of Finance (newly established), along with personnel from the Japanese military headquarters and armed soldiers, came to extract the salt tax revenue. They were told that money could not be withdrawn without a check. They replied that regardless of whether the audit office director allowed it or not, the money must be withdrawn today. If there were any problems, they would be responsible. If payment was refused, it would be regarded as intentional defiance. The arguments were ineffective, and at 4:00 PM, 672,709 yuan and 5 jiao and 6 fen were taken away. After several negotiations, Yamada issued a receipt. (Omitted below) Memorial (2) On November 3, a report was submitted. The following is a continuation: (1) The Changchun Audit Sub-Office telegraphed on the 6th, stating that all deposits in the Chinese Communications Banks today were forcibly submitted to the Changchun Dongsansheng Guanyin Bank with a notice signed solely by officials of the Monopoly Transportation Bureau and approved by the local foreign (Japanese) military authorities. Our protests were ineffective. The Monopoly Transportation Bureau officially notified the sub-office today, stating that the audit office was not recognized. (2) A telegram from the Yingkou commissioner reported that three foreigners (Japanese), one of whom was in military uniform, demanded the tax revenue of October 30. Later, three Chinese from the Guanyin Bank joined in, claiming that they were determined to extract the tax revenue collected by the Bank of China (Yingkou branch) daily, averaging about 45,000 yuan. According to the Changchun Sub-Office's previous report, the Changchun salt tax account had accumulated 2.6 million yuan by October 31. It is expected that the money extracted on the 6th will be added to the tax revenue collected by Jilin and Heilongjiang after the end of October (according to last night's telegram, 720,000 yuan was taken). This money was ordered by the newly appointed director of the Monopoly Transportation Bureau of the Local Maintenance Committee, backed by the Japanese occupying army. Furthermore, according to Yingkou, the decision to extract tax revenue daily will amount to 1.125 million yuan per month. The Japanese military authorities have stated that they accept the principle of allocating salt affairs expenses of 58,200 yuan per month and foreign debt apportionment of 217,800 yuan per month first, but do not recognize the repayment of arrears apportionment of 662,800 yuan per month. Now the salt tax revenue in the three northeastern provinces is extremely short. If 45,000 yuan is extracted daily on average, it will be impossible to cope with the monthly expenses and the amount due for foreign debt. The amount due for repayment of arrears will be even less. If the amount due for repayment of debts in various places cannot be fully allocated, the 1929 plan for reorganizing the salt tax-guaranteed foreign debt will face significant obstacles in implementation next year.

Northeast Petition Group Visited Hu and Wang Separately Yesterday

▲Hosted Various Sectors to Report on the Process ▲Going to Beijing Soon, Returning Northward

Feng Yong, Su Shangda, Gao Jianguo, Yan Baohang, Du Yijie, and other five representatives of the Northeast People's National Salvation Petition Group visited Hu Hanmin at Maisi Ai Road yesterday at 5:00 PM and talked for about an hour. After the representatives bid farewell, they went to visit Wang Jingwei at Xin Pushi Road and left at about 8:00 PM. At the YMCA on Sichuan Road, they hosted the press and various sectors. Su Shangda reported on the organization process of the Northeast People's National Salvation Petition Group and the petition situation in Shanghai in recent days, stating briefly that since the violent Japanese occupied various parts of the Northeast, the people of the Northeast, especially the intellectuals, have felt particularly painful in what they have seen and heard. They had no choice but to leave the Northeast and could not bear not to leave. Most of them gathered in Pingjin, where they organized the Northeast People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Group and established a branch in Tianjin. In addition to propaganda, there were also special tasks. In the current situation, all Chinese people recognize that the entire China should deal with foreign aggression. Therefore, the people of the Northeast are paying close attention to this peace conference, and the news reported by the newspapers in Pingjin all said that the hope was dim, and finally there was news of a breakdown. Therefore, they resolutely organized a large-scale petition group to go south, weeping like in the Qin court to the gentlemen of the peace conference. After the news spread, in one day, 3,000 to 4,000 people automatically signed up, and the limit was set at 620 people due to economic reasons. After arriving in Shanghai, they learned that the peace conference had ended and lost its target. They had no choice but to submit petitions to the representatives staying in Shanghai separately and inquire about the end of the peace conference. In recent days, due to handling the pass through the concession for the whole group, the concession authorities did not allow it. Therefore, at 5:00 PM today (i.e., yesterday), five representatives were elected to visit Hu and Wang. The responses were very satisfactory. Therefore, the task of coming to Shanghai has been completed. They are scheduled to go to Beijing for a petition soon and then return to the north. Thank you very much for the hospitality of various groups in Shanghai. The following is a record of the conversation between Hu Hanmin and the representatives of the petition group yesterday. (As for the conversation between the representatives of the group and Wang, Wang detailed the process of the peace conference and the diplomatic policy towards the Northeast. The words were similar to Wang's conversations with various sectors in recent days, so they are not repeated here.) (The representative asked) What is the situation of national peace and unity? (Hu replied) Regarding the peace and unity organization and the unified government, the representatives of both sides have discussed and reached results. These issues now need to be submitted to the Fourth National Congress for discussion of the methods of the preparatory meeting, and then wait for the handling of the fourth executive and supervisory committees. (Asked) What is your opinion on the disposal of the diplomatic problems of the three northeastern provinces? (Answer) Now, the most important thing for this problem is to immediately send personnel to recover the lost territory. However, what I don't understand is that Japan's verbal propaganda does not say that it wants to take it for itself, but our country ignores it and does not take it back quickly. Although there is a Northeast Recovery Committee recently, it seems to be related to one person. It must be known that if our country can officially send personnel to take back the lost territory, and Japan is unwilling to hand it over, it can prove Japan's aggressive ambition, and our country can also make some preparations to fight it out and preserve the Chinese nation. If we continue to perfunctorily shirk responsibility and hold an attitude of non-resistance and non-responsibility, we will see a great land of China that will not be ours. (Asked) Our country has no preparation. Even if we want to take back the lost territory, what if Japan is strong and domineering to the end and our country is not strong enough? (Answer) If it is true as you said, then the Republic of China can simply be given to others with hands tied. What is the point of trying to survive? The representatives then asked Mr. Hu to express that they would set off for Beijing today to petition the government authorities again and urge them to recover the three northeastern provinces.

Guangdong Representatives Leave Shanghai Today

▲But Wang and Wu Still Stay in Shanghai for a Short Stay

After the Beijing-Guangdong Peace and Unity Conference was declared over, the Beijing and Guangdong sides are now actively preparing for the convening of the Fourth National Congress. The three Guangdong representatives, Sun, Chen, and Li, who were sent back to Guangdong, are scheduled to leave Shanghai on the Queen of Asia at 2:00 PM today. Yesterday, the second central committee members Cheng Qian, Li Liejun, Xu Qian, and others specially visited the Guangdong representative Sun Zhesheng at the Sun residence in the French Concession and said that they would provide considerable assistance in the release of Deng Yanda. As for Li Jishen's return to Guangdong, it has not yet happened due to physical discomfort. The news from yesterday is recorded in the following sections:

▲Wang Jingwei's Important Letter to Sun Ke, Li Wenfan, Chen Youren, etc. Returning South Wang Jingwei, Wu Chaoshu, Zou Lu, and Zeng have sent a letter to the representatives of the Fourth National Congress. This letter must be published in Guangzhou. Wang Jingwei also has another letter to his comrades who have shared hardships with him for many years. The full text is disclosed as follows: All Comrades, This is for your information. The results of this peace conference have been described in detail in the joint telegram issued yesterday. I think you have seen it. I was ordered to stay in Shanghai and did not get to return to Guangzhou to gather with you. If you have any questions about the results of the peace conference, I cannot answer them face-to-face. I respectfully propose the following questions and answers: Question 1. According to the original draft of the telegram from both parties, it is advocated that a unified government should be produced by a unified conference. If this is the case, is it not inconsistent with the original advocacy? Answer: The so-called unified conference does not stipulate how its composition should be. Now, the first plenary meeting of the Fourth Central Committee has decided to amend the Organic Law of the National Government and reorganize the government. Therefore, the so-called unified conference will be replaced by the first plenary meeting of the Fourth Central Committee. Question 2. Why is it not decided immediately whether Mr. Chiang should step down? Answer: This is the focus of the dispute between the two sides. In the past, there was no way to resolve this dispute other than by military means. Now, it is resolved by political means. It must be known that the result of military solution is often that the military force of party A is eliminated, and the military force of party B replaces it. There is no other way to use it lightly. If political methods can solve it, why take military solutions? The first plenary meeting of the Fourth Central Committee decided to amend the Organic Law of the National Government and reorganize the government, which is the so-called method of political solution. The amendment to the Organic Law of the National Government is about the issue of the system, and the reorganization of the government is about the issue of personnel selection. As far as the issue of the system is concerned, the current meeting has decided on a draft of the reform of the central political system. If it can be implemented, it can liberate politics from the control of military forces. This is actually the first step in democratic politics. As far as the issue of personnel selection is concerned, it is expected that there will be two proposals at that time: Mr. Chiang's resignation and retention. These two proposals will be decided by the majority of the meeting and obeyed. Compared with deciding the personal advancement and retreat by the victory or defeat of the military, it is much more economical. If we want to make the Chinese political phenomenon enter the right track, there is no other way to replace military solutions with political solutions. The Financial Committee can refuse the burden of civil war, and all kinds of resolutions regarding political disputes and not lightly solving them with military force are all ways to prevent civil war. If our comrades of the party can faithfully implement them, then it is hoped that the period of political tutelage will not return to military administration and will gradually advance to constitutional government. The above two are just the big ones. In short, our party comrades have sacrificed so many lives and so much freedom in the past few years. Now, we can only continue to work hard to complete this task, restoring democratic centralization to the party and supporting democratic politics in the country. It all depends on this. Resistance to foreign powers and cultivation of the country's foundation also depend on this. I only hope that you will consider it and wish you peace. Wang Zhaoming respectfully, November 9.

They did not leave until after 5:00 PM.

Temporary Suspension of Coal Transport Price Increase on the Jiaoji Railway

▲To be implemented upon approval from the Executive Yuan

Regarding the price increase for coal transport on the Jiaoji Railway, after Shandong mine owners expressed their opposition and initiated a unified strike, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, considering that the boycott of Japanese coal relies on domestic coal supply and that further issues could lead to a coal shortage with significant ramifications, telegraphed the Ministry of Railways requesting cancellation of the price increase. Simultaneously, they telegraphed the Shandong merchants to resume coal transport. It is now reported that a considerable resolution has been reached. The Jiaoji Railway Bureau has agreed to temporarily suspend the proposed coal transport price increase. The telegrams from the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Railways are recorded below:

▲Telegram from the Ministry of Industry to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, forwarded to the Navigation Industry Association, Chinese Cotton Mill United Association, Silk Manufacturers Association, Chinese Seamen's Union, Reorganization Committee, Copper, Iron, and Machinery Association, Oil Press Association, Inland Steamer Association, Chinese Marine Engineers Union, and the Chinese Merchant Ship Masters Association: Your telegram dated the 30th has been received. This matter has been previously reported by the Shandong Zibo Zhangwei Mining and Coal Industry United Association, Shanghai Coal Industry Association, National Chamber of Commerce Federation, and China National Coal Production and Sales United Association, stating that the sudden increase in freight rates by the railway makes it difficult for coal merchants to bear the burden. They earnestly request prompt withdrawal of the order to maintain domestic coal supply and alleviate merchants' difficulties. The Ministry has informed the Ministry of Railways accordingly, stating that while domestic coal is being promoted and various ports are anticipating coal shortages, disputes regarding coal transport on the railway are undesirable. Increasing freight rates at this time seems inappropriate. Whether the Ministry of Railways can be instructed to withdraw the order or postpone the implementation date to avoid unsettling public sentiment is requested for consideration and handling. The current telegram presents the same situation and claims that the Ministry of Railways has been telegraphed separately. It is hoped that the Ministry of Railways will consolidate the cases for review and handling. Sincerely, Ministry of Industry.

▲Reply from the Ministry of Railways, dated the 30th: Your telegram has been received. The coal freight rate on the Jiaoji Railway was appropriately reduced during the summer period at the request of various merchants, as instructed by the Ministry. Now that the reduced price period has expired, a fair special price has been re-established. This was pre-scheduled and implemented on time and is not a separate case. All railways are handling this simultaneously, not just the Jiaoji Railway alone. As for the excessive cost of Shandong coal, there are other reasons, certainly not due to the Jiaoji Railway freight rates. The Ministry has already explained this meticulously in a previous telegram to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. Regarding the current telegram and the request from various organizations to temporarily retain the price increase proposal, this is in line with the Ministry's current approach of temporarily setting coal transport price increases for various railways. Once approved by the Executive Yuan, it will be implemented immediately. Whether Shandong coal can fully supply Shanghai's coal shortage and whether the pricing can maintain the current state after the temporary suspension of the price increase, preventing both the railway bureau and users from suffering while coal merchants and transporters alone profit, depends entirely on the strict supervision and correction from all sectors. Otherwise, the facts will be evident, and it is impossible for a few individuals to deceive the world. This is hereby approved and notified.

Current Status of Resumption of Operations of Domestic Vessels on Rivers and Seas

▲Yangtze River, North and South Seas routes

▲Approximately 60 domestic vessels currently in operation

▲18 Japanese vessels remain on rivers and seas

Since the boycott, Japanese ships on rivers and seas have completely ceased operations. Even if they are running, they have no business. Cargo on various routes is abundant, but ships are scarce, allowing British ships to take the opportunity to rise. In September and October, Jardine Matheson and Butterfield & Swire each profited between one and two million. Since last month, when domestic shipping companies such as China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and San Peh Steam Navigation Company submitted a request to headquarters to allow ships to resume operations, they have been gradually returning to Shanghai and successively starting schedules. Today, domestic vessels on various river and sea routes can fully operate. The recent situation of shipping is recorded separately as follows:

▲Full operation of ships on the upper and lower Yangtze River. Chinese vessels on the Yangtze River, returned to China Merchants and San Peh in late October, are successively resuming operations. Currently, only the Jiangyu, Yongxing, and Jiangtian vessels are still being rented by the Transportation Department on the Shanghai-Hankou line. The rest have been returned to their respective shipping bureaus. Therefore, Yangtze River schedules now include the Jiang'an, Jiangshun, Xinjiang, Jianghua, Jiangjing, Jiangda, Jianguo, Xinning, Changxing, Dexing, Fulong, Chang'an, and Ningshao vessels. In the upper reaches, as the Kuaili, Emei, and Fuyang vessels have been returned, the Yichang, Changsha, and Chongqing schedules are all operating. More than ten vessels are in operation, including the Guangji, Liji, Hongyuan, Hongheng, Hongli, Hongzhen, and Wuxing. China Merchants is further expanding its upper Yangtze shipping business and has added two new large tugs and barges to the Hunan route. Currently, there are 26 Chinese river vessels operating on the upper and lower Yangtze River.

▲Smooth operations on North and South Sea routes. On the Guangzhou route of the South Sea line, since China Merchants dispatched the Yuan'an vessel, it is currently the peak season for loading goods such as beans, kernels, and cloth. It is regrettable that there are no additional vessels available. Additional schedules will be added once the ocean vessels rented by headquarters are returned. However, Zhengji Company has transferred four vessels in the North Sea to directly operate from Niuzhuang to various ports in the South Sea. In North China, China Merchants has two vessels operating between Yantai and Tianjin, and two vessels operating between Dalian and Yingkou. Zhaoxing and Zhengji each have three or four vessels traveling between Yantai, Yingkou, Tianjin, and Shanghai. To transport domestic coal, China Merchants and others will dispatch several ocean vessels to Qindao to transport coal. Zeng Guangqing, Chief of the Business Department of China Merchants, is taking this opportunity to go to Hong Kong to personally purchase two vessels to operate shipping. The first vessel has arrived, and the second will arrive in Shanghai soon, dispatching them to the North and South Seas to load cargo.

▲New domestic vessels added on the Shanghai-Fuzhou route. China Merchants, San Peh, and Chang'an each have one vessel operating on the Shanghai-Fuzhou route. Osaka Shosen Kaisha has three vessels traveling back and forth. Since the current boycott of goods began, merchants in Fujian have also unanimously refused to load Japanese ships. Starting this month, dockworkers and barge workers in Fuzhou have agreed not to load or unload goods from Japanese ships. Therefore, although Japanese ships are sailing, they have no business. Recently, when Fujian goods were congested, China Merchants' Guangli suddenly suspended operations for repairs. Customers urgently requested ships and sent telegrams to Shanghai. The Zhejiang Shipping Bureau of this city seized this opportunity to add a Shanghai-Fuzhou schedule, dispatching the Deli vessel from yesterday to Fuzhou to meet the demands of Fujian merchants.

▲Cargo congestion and increased fees on various routes. Starting this month, since domestic vessels have started operating on the Yangtze River, the export cargo of Butterfield & Swire and Jardine Matheson is no longer as congested as last month. However, the daily freight rate per vessel for transshipment cargo is still over 10,000. The China Merchants Jianglun has recently experienced unprecedentedly good business in the upper reaches, with freight exceeding 10,000 taels per vessel. Passenger traffic is even greater, with almost every vessel filled. Freight rates for upstream cargo have increased by 15%, with sugar, grain, oil, and cloth being the major cargo. The supply of downstream cargo is severely lacking. In the North Sea routes, flour, paper, and cloth are the major cargo, and freight rates have also increased due to cargo congestion. Beans and kernels are the major cargo in the South Sea routes. Currently, there are more than 30 Chinese ocean vessels operating in the North and South Seas. Combined with the Chinese merchant ships on both the rivers and seas, there are approximately 60 vessels currently in operation, an increase of approximately 40 vessels compared to last month. As for the Japanese vessels that have not suspended operations, there are currently 4 vessels on the Yangtze River, 4 vessels of Nisshin Kisen Kaisha in the North and South Seas, 3 vessels of Osaka Shosen Kaisha, 5 vessels of Dalian Kisen Kaisha, and 2 vessels of Kawasaki Kisen Kaisha, totaling 18 vessels, but there is nothing to speak of in terms of business.

Yesterday's News from the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association

▲Warning to Zhenfeng and Huatong Against Selling Japanese Goods. The Anti-Japanese Association of Shanghai sent a letter to Zhenfeng Trading Company and Huatong Electric Factory yesterday, stating: "To whom it may concern, previously, we received confidential reports that Zhenfeng Trading Company on the Bund and Huatong Electric Factory in Yangshupu were exclusively selling Japanese goods. We requested an investigation. After investigation, it was reported that Zhenfeng Trading Company, located upstairs of the Japanese Masui Yoko on the Bund, is indeed exclusively selling Japanese goods and is registered under a Japanese name with the consulate. Huatong Electric Factory in Yangshupu disguises and sells the goods, which is also a fact, and is related to Zhenfeng. Therefore, since the outbreak of the Japanese disaster, which has been ongoing for 50 days, the boycott of enemy goods and non-cooperation with the Japanese is a major plan for our entire nation to save itself. However, your companies, on one hand, rely on the enemy for protection, and on the other hand, deceive the domestic market, colluding with each other. You disregard the country's demise and the extinction of the race as insignificant. Your conscience is gone. Based on the above, we hereby issue a serious warning. If you fail to repent immediately and sever your relationship with the Japanese, this Association will fulfill its duties, and our compatriots will exercise their public opinion. Do not regret it later." Addressed to Zhenfeng Trading Company and Huatong Electric Factory.

▲Telegram to Hankou Urging Thorough Boycott of Japanese Coal. The Anti-Japanese Association telegraphed the Hankou Anti-Japanese Association, stating: "To the Hankou Anti-Japanese Association, the Coal Industry Association reported that since the anti-Japanese movement, Shanghai's industry has absolutely boycotted Japanese coal. We hear that Hankou has a method of allowing passage for a fee per ton, which may set a bad precedent for Shanghai's industry. Please telegraph the Hankou Anti-Japanese Association to jointly and thoroughly boycott it, and do not collect fees for passage to show consistency. It is important to be thorough in boycotting Japanese goods and actively carry it out. There should be no flexibility. Based on the above report, we hereby telegraph you, hoping you will take note. Sincerely, the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association."

Inspection of Japanese Goods by the Clothing Industry Association

▲Work Began Yesterday

After the establishment of the Japanese Goods Inspection Group of the Shanghai Clothing Industry Association, the standing committee members Wu Zhihao, Lu Qisheng, Hao Haishan, Yin Jiefu, Xi Xiaoyun, and others convened inspectors from various districts to decide on the plan. The plan divides the city into six districts: South Shanghai, North Shanghai, the Public Concession, the French Concession, West Shanghai, Xinzha, Caojiadu, East Shanghai Hongkou, and Yangshupu, totaling six districts. Thirty-six inspectors were designated to work together with workers in their respective areas. The South Shanghai district set off at 2:00 PM yesterday, with Xi Xiaoyun, Yao Guifang, Wu Jinxian, and other workers conducting inspections in the city, the Sixteenth Ward, Limma Road, and the Third Street. They inspected the few Japanese goods in various stores and sealed them up. They also inspected the Tonghe New Clothing Store on Wangjia Wharf, where the owner Gao Jingchuan was found cutting and sewing clothes with Japanese raw materials. The committee members seized the goods and sealed them up temporarily, intending to report it to the Anti-Japanese Association for punishment.

Local News II

A Major Tragedy in a Fire: Eleven People Burned to Death

▲Fire Breaks Out at Pengfuji Optical Shop

▲Spreads to as many as 29 Houses

▲The Faces of the Dead are Unrecognizably Blurred

▲The Number of Victims May Be More Than This

At 1:10 AM yesterday morning, a fire suddenly broke out at the Pengfuji Optical Shop, located at No. 26 Fuxing Lane, Zhangjia Lane, Sanpailou, Nanshi. The fire lasted for one hour and thirty minutes, and was finally extinguished at 2:45 AM. The fire destroyed eight neighboring houses and burned ten people to death. One person was injured and died without medical treatment. Several people were seriously injured. It was a major tragedy in a fire. The details are recorded below:

▲A Family of Twenty-Eight. Peng Fuquan, a 42-year-old man from Danyang, has been running Pengfuji Optical Shop at No. 26 Fuxing Lane, Zhangjia Lane, Sanpailou, Nanshi, for many years. The business is quite prosperous. Including children, partners, and apprentices, there are a total of 28 people in the family. Peng's wife, Bian, is 38 years old and has two sons and two daughters. The eldest daughter, Suodi, is 13 years old, the second son, Suohong, is 11 years old, the third daughter, Suoying, is 4 years old, and the youngest son, Suoxi, is only 2 years old.

▲List of Partners' Names. Because the business is prosperous, Peng employs a total of more than 20 workers, partners, and apprentices, including Zhu Quanfu, 17 years old, Xu Yulin, 32 years old, Wang Chunlong, 34 years old, Sui Sheshun, 21 years old, Hu Tongqing, 23 years old, Yin Fashun, 20 years old, Yin Koulong, 26 years old, Jiang Linlin, 18 years old, Liu Lachun, 29 years old, Xiao Tiefang, 27 years old, Xie Fulong, 27 years old (all from Danyang), A Si, 26 years old, Wu Helin, 28 years old, Peng Yongsheng, 27 years old, Jiang Heshun, 30 years old, Wang Guilin, 20 years old, Liu Panquan, 23 years old, Tao Achun, 18 years old, Ni Siming, 22 years old, Lv Ageng, 33 years old (all from Wuxi), Zhuang Chunsheng, 25 years old, and Lu Ada, 23 years old (both from Suzhou).

▲Fire Suddenly Breaks Out in the Middle of the Night. Because the house is narrow and there are many people, in addition to the original houses being insufficient, two lofts were added on the upper floor to serve as dormitories for workers and apprentices. At 1:10 AM yesterday morning, when the whole family was fast asleep, the remaining fire was accidentally left in the rosin raw material used for making glasses, causing a fire. When the people woke up and realized it, they were already enveloped in thick smoke and fainted in the fire. In addition, it was late at night, and no one knew about it. It was not until the fire broke through the roof that people learned about it. However, the situation had already spread and could not be saved.

▲Mistress Jumps Out of Window and is Injured. At that time, Peng and his wife, Bian, jumped out of the window and were seriously injured. The fire brigades in the Nanshi districts drove to the scene one after another to assist in the rescue. A firefighter bravely rushed into the fire and rescued a partner, Peng Yongsheng. Peng was burned all over his body and was sent to Shanghai Nanyang Hospital by ambulance. Due to severe injuries, he died in the hospital at 8:00 AM yesterday. The hospital notified the second branch of the first district, which instructed the bailiff Huang Baoyuan to report to the local court for inspection.

▲Involved Twenty-Nine Families. The fire destroyed a total of eight houses. In addition to No. 26, where the fire started, there were the houses of Hua Aju, a Wuxi man selling chicken and duck blood at No. 24, Zhou Changyu, a Wuxi man at No. 25, Chen Dalang, a Chongming man at No. 27, Wang Zhao, a Shaoxing woman at No. 28, Guan Chunsheng, a Hangzhou man at No. 32, Ge Jintang, a Nanjing man at No. 33, and Xu Xianglin, a Haimen man at No. 34. Including the three tenants, there were a total of 29 families.

▲Ten Corpses. The scene was tragic. When the fire was raging, Yi, the head of the second branch of the first district, supervised all the police officers and the fire brigade to try to rescue them. After searching, Peng Fuquan, the owner of the first fire, was missing. After the fire was completely extinguished, it was already dawn. The firefighters cleaned up the remaining embers, and unexpectedly, ten bodies were successively pulled out from the fire at No. 26, all burned into charred bones, and placed on the side of the road. The faces were blurred and unrecognizable. The scene was so tragic that it made people feel sad. As for who was killed and who was spared, because the owner Peng Fuquan is still unknown, it is impossible to investigate clearly for a while. As for whether there were any victims in the other neighboring houses, the ashes are still being dug up.

▲Labor Unions Raise Funds to Collect Corpses. After the bodies were pulled out, Yi, the head of the second branch of the first district, immediately instructed the bailiff Huang Baoyuan to petition the local court for inspection. At 5:00 PM yesterday, Prosecutor Wu Shixin and Clerk Qian, as well as Inspector Shen, arrived at the scene and inspected a total of eleven bodies, all of which were burned to death. The names could not be identified for a while. The district heads were ordered to guard them temporarily. It is heard that a certain labor union will raise funds to collect them.

Various Labor Unions Pay Attention to the You Bolu Case

▲Entrust Lawyer Mao Yun to Appear in Court for Defense

▲Appoint Representatives to Attend and Observe

The local court has scheduled a hearing for the case of You Bolu's massacre of the masses during his tenure as the chief of the Fifth District of the Public Security Bureau at 10:00 AM today. The various labor unions in this city have entrusted the barrister Mao Yun to appear in court to defend him according to the law. Seven Kidnappers in the Zhu Yanqing Case Sentenced to Death

▲Tang Afu Sentenced to Life Imprisonment

▲Cao Zhang Sentenced to Twelve Years

Zhu Yanqing, the young owner of the Zhenhe Tea Shop in De'an Lane, North Shanxi Road, Anhui Province, was kidnapped by kidnappers at about 11:00 PM on September 8 when he was taking a chartered car home. He was taken to a pavilion room at No. 73 Jianye Lane, Fulili Road, French Concession, in an attempt to extort a huge ransom. After investigation by detective Jin Jiulin and patrol detectives of the French Police, they rescued Zhu on the 15th of the month and arrested 12 men and women, including Zheng A'er, Yu Aqing, Tang Afu, Qian Daoyuan, Hong Aji, Lu Yisheng, Wang Ziqing, Liu Shaoqing, robber Cao Zhang, Zhao Liu, and Wang Jiang. They seized firearms, bullets, glasses, iron chains, and other items, and took them to the police station and escorted them to the Criminal Court of the Second Special District Local Court. After repeated interrogations by Judge Luo Renji and Prosecutor Ding Shikui, the defendants confessed to kidnapping and attempting to extort ransom. The court appointed lawyers Wang Shizong, Xu Yannian, Lin Yingqing, Gu Changyuan, Wu Youyuan, and others to defend the defendants. The court announced the conclusion of the trial and waited for the verdict. Yesterday was the date of the verdict. At 10:00 AM, the police escorted the defendants to the court. Judge Luo ordered the defendants to be brought to the First Criminal Court and announced the verdict. The main text of the verdict was: Zheng A'er, Qian Daoyuan, Lu Yisheng, Liu Shaoqing, Yu Aqing, and Hong A'gen were each sentenced to death for the crime of extortion. Tang Afu was sentenced to life imprisonment for the crime of kidnapping and extortion. Cao Zhang was sentenced to 12 years of imprisonment for the crime of kidnapping and extortion. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined to be one day of imprisonment for every two days. Two pistols, 14 bullets, two bullet casings, one iron chain, one lock, one iron chisel, and one pair of black glasses were confiscated. Zhao Liu and Wang Jiang were acquitted.

Iron Shop Owner's Young Son Kidnapped

▲ Shop Owner's Cousin and a Shop Employee Conspire ▲ After the Case is Solved, a Letter Demands 50,000 Yuan Ransom

▲ Twelve Male and Female Bandits Arrested in Succession

Jiang Zirong, a Wuxi native residing at 529 Tiantong Road, runs the Yicheng Iron Shop. His life was reasonably good, and he had accumulated some savings. Jiang's seven-year-old son, Jiabao, was intelligent and handsome, and he was cherished like a pearl in the palm of the hand. Suddenly, at 2:30 PM on the 7th of this month, he went missing without a trace. A thorough search yielded no results. Later, the shop apprentice, Zhu Asan, claimed that he had seen the shop employee Shen Quanbao's cousin, Shen Asan, also from Wuxi, leave with Jiabao, but he did not know where they were going to play. Shen Quanbao knew that his cousin Asan lived at 1 Sanyangli, Yangshupu Road, and secretly reported this to the Huishan Police Station. Chinese detectives Zhao Ruisheng and Ji Peijin, along with a Western detective, went to arrest Shen Asan around 1:00 AM the day before yesterday. They asked where the child was hidden, and he claimed it was at 263 Pingliang Road. Arriving there, they found three Ningbo natives, Yang Wenguang, Zhang Mingzhao, and Wei Senlin, living in the house. A search found no sign of Jiang's child. After questioning, they learned that the child was inside the house at 150 Lumingli, Huishan Road. They arrested Yang and the other two men and went to look for the child. A Ningbo native named Yu Arui said that he had seen a woman take the child away, at number 15 in the same alley. The detectives arrested him as well. They went to the house, broke down the door, and went upstairs, where they found Shaoxing women Qian Qius, Yang Wu (Yang Wenguang's wife), Qian Wang, and Jiang's child sleeping in the same bed. The women were awakened from their dreams and arrested one by one, and Jiang Jiabao was rescued. All were taken back to the police station. Afterward, detectives were stationed inside the houses at 15 and 150 Demingli, Huishan Road. They subsequently arrested four more people, including Ningbo natives Yu Zhulin, Wang Yuanlin, Qian Zhangyue (Qian Qiu's husband), and Shaoxing woman Zhu Jinfeng. Inside the house at number 15, under the bed, they found a live ammunition pistol and one hundred bullets in a lead teapot. In total, twelve male and female bandits were apprehended. The police chief ordered them to be detained separately. The child was taken back by his father, Jiang Zirong. Around 10:00 AM, the shop received a letter delivered by the post office addressed to the child's father, stating that 50,000 yuan was required for his return. The meeting place was to be near the Xiawang Bridge outside the Ningbo South Gate, with a 1,000 yuan deposit to be paid first, or the child would be killed. (This letter was sent before the case was solved.) Jiang Zirong immediately sent it to the police station for safekeeping. Yesterday morning, Shen Asan and the other twelve were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special Court. The police station's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated the case, saying that the police station was prosecuting the defendants for the crime of kidnapping. A letter was also found on the defendant Yu Zhulin, detailing that the meeting place had been changed to the Liangting Pavilion at the Yongduan Lin Bridge. The person coming to meet was to wear a red scarf around their waist, a red knot on their head, and a melon-shaped hat. According to what he said at the police station, this letter was a draft written by the defendant Qian Zhangyue at the China Hotel, number 91 Jiujiang Road. The two letters, as well as the gun, bullets, lead teapot, etc., were submitted for review, with a request for a postponement. Following this, the plaintiff Jiang Zirong submitted a petition describing the events. The shop employee Shen Quanbao and apprentice Zhu Asan also gave statements. The child, Jiang Jiabao, said that he had been tricked into going outside by the defendant Shen Asan to buy a machine bicycle, and they rode in a rickshaw to a house. He pointed out that the defendants Qian Qius, Yang Wu, Qian Wang, and the woman Zhu Jinfeng were all present. Yu Zhulin had also come. Yang Wu gave him cakes to eat, and he slept with Qian Qius and Yang Wu at night. Qian Wang and Zhu Jinfeng played with him during the day. After Judge Xiao Xieying questioned the defendants, their answers were mostly evasive. However, Shen Asan admitted that he had conspired with Yu Zhulin, Qian Zhangyue, and Qian Qius. Qian Zhangyue had provided 55 yuan for the gun, which Yu Zhulin bought from a certain bungalow on Pingliang Road. Judge Xiao then ordered the defendants to be returned to custody separately for further questioning at a later date.

Xue Guisheng Kidnapped and Interrogated

On the evening of the 3rd of this month, rumors spread that Guisheng, the third son of the deceased paint magnate Xue Baorun, had been kidnapped that afternoon at 3:00 PM, after his car drove near Julaida Road from his private residence on Masinan Road. When reporters heard this, they went to both the English and French police stations to investigate, but both police stations claimed that no kidnapping cases had occurred within their jurisdictions that day. The reporters then went to the Xue residence to inquire, but everyone there firmly denied it and said that nothing of the sort had happened. Out of caution at the time, it was not appropriate to disclose this rashly. However, as of yesterday, according to relatives and friends close to the Xue family, the young master was indeed kidnapped on the 3rd, but the family did not report it to the police and instructed everyone in the house to keep it strictly secret from outsiders, and to reject visits from news reporters. Based on this, it seems that Xue's kidnapping is a fact.

Planning Northwest Aviation

▲ Li Jingcong Went to Beiping Yesterday to Plan the Route

The Northwest air route, planned and developed by the Eurasia Aviation Corporation, is showing some progress. The company previously sent German engineer Smith, deputy director of the air navigation team, to Beiping to plan. Now, it has sent director Li Jingcong to Beiping yesterday morning to oversee the preparations. According to Sun Mutang, secretary of the company, speaking to a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency, there are currently no problems with the supply of gasoline. Although the Northwest is located in a remote area with nowhere to purchase gasoline, it can be supplied from British India on one hand, and can also be purchased from Russia on the other. However, because the Northwest's weather is severely cold, the gasoline stationed at each station may freeze and become unusable. Therefore, the company plans to keep the gasoline warm at each predetermined station to prevent it from freezing and hindering flights.

▲ To be Implemented on November 15th

The Jinghu, Huhangyong Railway Bureau recently received an order from the Ministry of Railways, setting a three-month limit starting from November 15th to surcharge a 10% disaster relief fee on first, second, and third-class passenger tickets where the fare is over 50 cents. Other tickets, such as fourth-class tickets, night train sleeper tickets, and special express train surcharges, are exempt from the surcharge.
